::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Vimānavatthupāḷi

### 1. Itthivimānaṃ

#### 1. Pīṭhavaggo

#### 1. Paṭhamapīṭhavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
{pb:T:0.0001} ‘‘Pīṭhaṃ {pb:M:0.0001}{pb:V:0.0001}{pb:P:0.0001} te sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkate malyadhare {note:mālyadhare (syā.)} suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:V:0.0002} taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena {note:moggalānena (ka.) evamuparipi} pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ {pb:T:0.0002} puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:M:0.0002} manussesu manussabhūtā, abbhāgatānāsanakaṃ adāsiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ, yathānubhāvañca adāsi dānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamapīṭhavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Dutiyapīṭhavimānavatthu

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ {pb:P:0.0002} te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkate malyadhare suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi {pb:T:0.0003} evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, abbhāgatānāsanakaṃ adāsiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ, yathānubhāvañca adāsi dānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:0.0003} metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi {pb:V:0.0003} te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Dutiyapīṭhavimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Tatiyapīṭhavimānavatthu

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ {pb:P:0.0003} te sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkate malyadhare suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti {pb:T:0.0004} ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ {note:mametaṃ (ka.)}, yenamhi {note:tenamhi (ka.)} evaṃ jalitānubhāvā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addasaṃ {pb:M:0.0004} virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa adāsahaṃ pīṭhaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Tatiyapīṭhavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Catutthapīṭhavimānavatthu

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ {pb:T:0.0005}{pb:P:0.0004} te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;

::gatha1

#### 5. Kuñjaravimānavatthu

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuñjaro {pb:P:0.0005} te varāroho, nānāratanakappano;
::

::gathalast
Ruciro thāmavā javasampanno, ākāsamhi samīhati.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumi padma {note:paduma… (sī. syā.) evamuparipi} pattakkhi, padmuppalajutindharo;
::

::gathalast
Padmacuṇṇābhikiṇṇaṅgo, soṇṇapokkharamāladhā {note:… mālavā (sī. syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumānusaṭaṃ maggaṃ, padmapattavibhūsitaṃ.
::

::gathalast
Ṭhitaṃ vaggumanugghātī, mitaṃ gacchati vāraṇo.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa pakkamamānassa, soṇṇakaṃsā ratissarā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa nāgassa khandhamhi, sucivatthā alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Mahantaṃ accharāsaṅghaṃ, vaṇṇena atirocasi.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānassa {pb:V:0.0005} te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
::

::gathalast
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchitā’’ti;
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna {pb:T:0.0007}{pb:M:0.0006} guṇasampannaṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ sataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adāsiṃ pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ, āsanaṃ dussasanthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaḍḍhaṃ padmamālāhaṃ, āsanassa samantato;
::

::gathalast
Abbhokirissaṃ pattehi, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa kammakusalassa {note:kammassa kusalassa (sī. pī.)}, idaṃ me īdisaṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkāro garukāro ca, devānaṃ apacitā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ve sammāvimuttānaṃ, santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pasanno āsanaṃ dajjā, evaṃ nande yathā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi attakāmena {note:atthakāmena (ka.)}, mahattamabhikaṅkhatā;
::

::gathalast
Āsanaṃ dātabbaṃ hoti, sarīrantimadhārina’’nti.
::

::centre
Kuñjaravimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Paṭhamanāvāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ {pb:P:0.0006} nāvaṃ, nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi;
::

::gathalast
Ogāhasi pokkharaṇiṃ, padmaṃ {note:padumaṃ (sī. syā.)} chindasi pāṇinā.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi {pb:T:0.0008} evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:M:0.0007} manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna bhikkhū tasite kilante, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:V:0.0006} ve kilantāna pipāsitānaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
::

::gathalast
Sītodakā {note:sītodikā (sī.)} tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ āpagā {note:tamāpagā (sī. ka.)} anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
::

::gathalast
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassīdha {note:tasseva (syā.)} kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā {note:katapuññā (sī.)} labhanti.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:0.0009} metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamanāvāvimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast

56\.

::hangnum
57\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Disvāna bhikkhuṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ve kilantassa pipāsitassa, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
::

::gathalast
Sītodakā tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
::

::gathalast
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:V:0.0007} bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassīdha kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi {pb:T:0.0011}{pb:M:0.0009} te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.

::centre

#### 8. Tatiyanāvāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ {pb:P:0.0008} nāvaṃ, nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi;
::

::gathalast
Ogāhasi pokkharaṇiṃ, padmaṃ chindasi pāṇinā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgārā {pb:P:0.0009} nivesā te, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
::

::gathalast
Daddallamānā {note:daddaḷhamānā (ka.)} ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, sambuddheneva pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna {pb:T:0.0012} bhikkhū tasite kilante, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ve kilantāna pipāsitānaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
::

::gathalast
Sītodakā tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:0.0010} āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
::

::gathalast
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassīdha kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgārā {pb:V:0.0008} nivesā me, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
::

::gathalast
Daddallamānā ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te buddha mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Etassa {pb:T:0.0013} kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ, atthāya buddho udakaṃ apāyī’’ti {note:apāsīti (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::centre
Tatiyanāvāvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.

{para:136} 136\. ‘‘Mama {pb:M:0.0018} ca, bhante, vacanena bhagavato pāde sirasā vandeyyāsi – ‘uttarā nāma, bhante, upāsikā bhagavato pāde sirasā vandatī’ti. Anacchariyaṃ kho panetaṃ, bhante, yaṃ maṃ bhagavā aññatarasmiṃ sāmaññaphale byākareyya {note:byākareyyāti (?)}, taṃ bhagavā sakadāgāmiphale byākāsī’’ti.

#### 16. Sirimāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yuttā {pb:P:0.0017} ca te paramaalaṅkatā hayā, adhomukhā aghasigamā balī javā;
::

::gathalast
Abhinimmitā pañcarathāsatā ca te, anventi taṃ sārathicoditā hayā.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā tiṭṭhasi rathavare alaṅkatā, obhāsayaṃ jalamiva joti pāvako;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ varatanu {note:varacāru (katthaci)} anomadassane, kasmā nu kāyā anadhivaraṃ upāgami.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmaggapattānaṃ {pb:V:0.0014} yamāhunuttaraṃ {note:… nuttarā (ka.), anuttarā (syā.)}, nimmāya nimmāya ramanti devatā;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā kāyā accharā kāmavaṇṇinī, idhāgatā anadhivaraṃ namassituṃ.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure sucaritamācarīdha {note:sucaritaṃ acāridha (pī.)},
::

::gatha2
Kenacchasi {pb:T:0.0023} tvaṃ amitayasā sukhedhitā;
::

::gatha3
Iddhī ca te anadhivarā vihaṅgamā,
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇo ca te dasa disā virocati.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devehi tvaṃ parivutā sakkatā casi,
::

::gatha2
Kuto cutā sugatigatāsi devate;
::

::gatha3
Kassa vā tvaṃ vacanakarānusāsaniṃ,
::

::gathalast
Ācikkha me tvaṃ yadi buddhasāvikā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nagantare {pb:M:0.0019} nagaravare sumāpite, paricārikā rājavarassa sirimato;
::

::gathalast
Nacce gīte paramasusikkhitā ahuṃ, sirimāti maṃ rājagahe avediṃsu {note:avedisuṃ (?)}.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho ca me isinisabho vināyako, adesayī samudayadukkhaniccataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asaṅkhataṃ dukkhanirodhasassataṃ, maggañcimaṃ akuṭilamañjasaṃ sivaṃ.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvānahaṃ amatapadaṃ asaṅkhataṃ, tathāgatassanadhivarassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīlesvahaṃ paramasusaṃvutā ahuṃ, dhamme ṭhitā naravarabuddhadesite {note:bhāsite (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ñatvānahaṃ virajapadaṃ asaṅkhataṃ, tathāgatenanadhivarena {pb:T:0.0024} desitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthevahaṃ samathasamādhimāphusiṃ, sāyeva me paramaniyāmatā ahu.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Laddhānahaṃ {pb:P:0.0018} amatavaraṃ visesanaṃ, ekaṃsikā abhisamaye visesiya;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃsayā bahujanapūjitā ahaṃ, khiḍḍāratiṃ {note:khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ (syā. pī.)} paccanubhomanappakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ ahaṃ amatadasamhi {note:amatarasamhi (ka.)} devatā, tathāgatassanadhivarassa sāvikā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaddasā paṭhamaphale patiṭṭhitā, sotāpannā na ca pana matthi duggati.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā vandituṃ anadhivaraṃ upāgamiṃ, pāsādike kusalarate ca bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Namassituṃ samaṇasamāgamaṃ sivaṃ, sagāravā sirimato dhammarājino.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā {pb:M:0.0020} muniṃ muditamanamhi pīṇitā, tathāgataṃ naravaradammasārathiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhacchidaṃ kusalarataṃ vināyakaṃ, vandāmahaṃ paramahitānukampaka’’nti.
::

::centre
Sirimāvimānaṃ soḷasamaṃ.
::

#### 17. Kesakārīvimānavatthu

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:T:0.0025}{pb:V:0.0015}{pb:P:0.0019} vimānaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, veḷuriyathambhaṃ satataṃ sunimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇarukkhehi samantamotthataṃ, ṭhānaṃ mamaṃ kammavipākasambhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatrūpapannā purimaccharā imā, sataṃ sahassāni sakena kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Tuvaṃsi ajjhupagatā yasassinī, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhasi pubbadevatā.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasī adhiggayha yathā virocati, nakkhattarājāriva tārakāgaṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva tvaṃ accharāsaṅgaṇaṃ {note:accharāsaṅgamaṃ (sī.)} imaṃ, daddallamānā yasasā virocasi.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuto nu āgamma anomadassane, upapannā tvaṃ bhavanaṃ mamaṃ idaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brahmaṃva devā tidasā sahindakā, sabbe na tappāmase dassanena ta’’nti.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yametaṃ sakka anupucchase mamaṃ, ‘kuto cutā tvaṃ idha āgatā’ti {note:kuto cutā idha āgatā tuvaṃ (syā.), kuto cutāya āgati tava (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bārāṇasī nāma puratthi kāsinaṃ, tattha ahosiṃ pure kesakārikā.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhe {pb:T:0.0026}{pb:M:0.0021} ca dhamme ca pasannamānasā, saṅghe ca ekantagatā asaṃsayā;
::

::gathalast
Akhaṇḍasikkhāpadā āgatapphalā, sambodhidhamme niyatā anāmayā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tantyābhinandāmase svāgatañca {note:sāgatañca (sī.)} te, dhammena ca tvaṃ yasasā virocasi;
::

::gatha2
Buddhe ca dhamme ca pasannamānase, saṅghe ca ekantagate asaṃsaye;
::

::gathalast
Akhaṇḍasikkhāpade āgatapphale, sambodhidhamme niyate anāmaye’’ti.
::

::centre
Kesakārīvimānaṃ sattarasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Pīṭhavaggo paṭhamo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Pañca pīṭhā tayo nāvā, dīpatiladakkhiṇā dve;
::

::gatha2
Pati dve suṇisā uttarā, sirimā kesakārikā;
::

::gathalast
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
::

#### 2. Cittalatāvaggo

#### 1. Dāsivimānavatthu

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Api {pb:V:0.0016}{pb:P:0.0021} sakkova devindo, ramme cittalatāvane;
::

::gatha2
Samantā anupariyāsi, nārīgaṇapurakkhatā;
::

::gathalast
Obhāsentī {pb:T:0.0027} disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:M:0.0022} taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;

::gathalast

160\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
161\.

162\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akaṇṭako agahano, uju sabbhi pavedito;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmantanikā raññomhi, sakkassa vasavattino;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhi {pb:P:0.0022} turiya {note:turiya (sī. syā. pī.)} sahassāni, paṭibodhaṃ karonti me.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ālambo gaggaro {note:gaggamo (syā.), bhaggaro (ka.)} bhīmo {note:bhimmo (ka.)}, sādhuvādī ca saṃsayo;
::

::gathalast
Pokkharo {pb:T:0.0028} ca suphasso ca, viṇāmokkhā {note:vilāmokkhā (ka.)} ca nāriyo.
::

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandā ceva sunandā ca, soṇadinnā sucimhitā {note:sucimbhikā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Alambusā missakesī ca, puṇḍarīkāti dāruṇī.
::

::hangnum
168\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eṇīphassā suphassā ca, subhaddā muduvādinī;
::

::gathalast
Etā caññā ca seyyāse, accharānaṃ pabodhikā.
::

::hangnum
169\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā {pb:V:0.0017} maṃ kālenupāgantvā, abhibhāsanti devatā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nayidaṃ {pb:M:0.0023} akatapuññānaṃ, katapuññānamevidaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, idha natthi parattha ca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ sahabyakāmānaṃ, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katapuññā hi modanti, sagge bhogasamaṅgino’’ti.
::

::centre
Dāsivimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 4. Caṇḍālivimānavatthu

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

196\.

‘‘Abhippasādehi manaṃ, arahantamhi tādini {note:tādine (syā. ka.)};

::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
220\.

::gatha1

#### 3. Pāricchattakavaggo

#### 1. Uḷāravimānavatthu

::

288\.
::

::

292\.

::gathalast

293\.

#### 2. Ucchudāyikāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
296\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Obhāsayitvā {pb:V:0.0027}{pb:P:0.0037} pathaviṃ {note:paṭhaviṃ (sī. syā.)} sadevakaṃ, atirocasi candimasūriyā viya;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
297\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ uppalamāladhārinī, āveḷinī kañcanasannibhattace;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
298\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūtā purimāya jātiyā;
::

::gatha2
Dānaṃ suciṇṇaṃ atha sīlasaṃyamaṃ {note:saññamaṃ (sī.)}, kenūpapannā {pb:T:0.0042} sugatiṃ yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
299\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idāni {pb:M:0.0035} bhante imameva gāmaṃ {note:gāme (syā. ka.)}, piṇḍāya amhākaṃ gharaṃ upāgami;
::

::gathalast
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā.
::

::hangnum
300\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sassu ca pacchā anuyuñjate mamaṃ, kahaṃ {note:kahaṃ me (pī.)} nu ucchuṃ vadhuke avākiri {note:avākari (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Na chaḍḍitaṃ no pana khāditaṃ mayā, santassa bhikkhussa sayaṃ adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
301\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyhaṃnvidaṃ {note:tuyhaṃ nu idaṃ (syā.)} issariyaṃ atho mama, itissā sassu paribhāsate mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pīṭhaṃ gahetvā pahāraṃ adāsi me, tato cutā kālakatāmhi devatā.
::

::hangnum
302\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
::

::hangnum
303\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
304\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisaṃ puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahāvipākā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
::

::gathalast
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
::

::hangnum
305\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisaṃ {pb:P:0.0038} puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahājutikā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
306\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvañca {pb:M:0.0036} bhante anukampakaṃ viduṃ, upecca vandiṃ kusalañca pucchisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacitā atulāya pītiyā’’ti.

#### 3. Pallaṅkavimānavatthu

::hangnum
307\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pallaṅkaseṭṭhe {pb:V:0.0028}{pb:P:0.0039} maṇisoṇṇacitte, pupphābhikiṇṇe sayane uḷāre;
::

::gathalast
Tatthacchasi devi mahānubhāve, uccāvacā iddhi vikubbamānā.
::

::hangnum
308\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imā ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti {pb:T:0.0044} gāyanti pamodayanti;
::

::gatha2
Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
309\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, aḍḍhe kule suṇisā ahosiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkodhanā bhattuvasānuvattinī, uposathe appamattā ahosiṃ {note:appamattā uposathe (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
310\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manussabhūtā daharā apāpikā {note:daharāsa’pāpikā (sī.)}, pasannacittā patimābhirādhayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Divā ca ratto ca manāpacārinī, ahaṃ pure sīlavatī ahosiṃ.
::

::hangnum
311\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipātā {pb:M:0.0037} viratā acorikā, saṃsuddhakāyā sucibrahmacārinī;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapā no ca musā abhāṇiṃ, sikkhāpadesu paripūrakārinī.
::

::hangnum
312\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, pasannamānasā ahaṃ {note:atipasannamānasā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
313\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhaṅgupetaṃ anudhammacārinī, uposathaṃ {pb:T:0.0045} pītimanā upāvasiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Imañca ariyaṃ aṭṭhaṅgavarehupetaṃ, samādiyitvā kusalaṃ sukhudrayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Patimhi kalyāṇī vasānuvattinī, ahosiṃ pubbe sugatassa sāvikā.
::

::hangnum
314\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisaṃ kusalaṃ jīvaloke, kammaṃ karitvāna visesabhāginī;
::

::gathalast
Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, deviddhipattā sugatimhi āgatā.
::

::hangnum
315\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vimānapāsādavare manorame, parivāritā accharāsaṅgaṇena;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃpabhā devagaṇā ramenti maṃ, dīghāyukiṃ devavimānamāgata’’nti;
::

::centre
Pallaṅkavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Latāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
316\.
::

::gatha1
Latā {pb:P:0.0040} ca sajjā pavarā ca devatā, accimatī {note:accimukhī (sī.), acchimatī (pī. ka.) acchimutī (syā.)} rājavarassa sirīmato;
::

::gathalast
Sutā ca rañño vessavaṇassa dhītā, rājīmatī dhammaguṇehi sobhatha.
::

::hangnum
317\.
::

::gatha1
Pañcettha {pb:V:0.0029}{pb:M:0.0038} nāriyo āgamaṃsu nhāyituṃ, sītodakaṃ uppaliniṃ sivaṃ nadiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tā {pb:T:0.0046} tattha nhāyitvā rametvā devatā, naccitvā gāyitvā sutā lataṃ bravi {note:bruvī (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
318\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ uppalamāladhārini, āveḷini kañcanasannibhattace;
::

::gathalast
Timiratambakkhi nabheva sobhane, dīghāyukī kena kato yaso tava.
::

::hangnum
319\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenāsi bhadde patino piyatarā, visiṭṭhakalyāṇitarassu rūpato;
::

::gathalast
Padakkhiṇā naccagītavādite, ācikkha no tvaṃ naranāripucchitā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
320\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, uḷārabhoge kule suṇisā ahosiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkodhanā bhattuvasānuvattinī, uposathe appamattā ahosiṃ.
::

::hangnum
321\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manussabhūtā {pb:P:0.0041} daharā apāpikā {note:daharāsa’pāpikā (sī.)}, pasannacittā patimābhirādhayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sadevaraṃ sassasuraṃ sadāsakaṃ, abhirādhayiṃ tamhi kato yaso mama.
::

::hangnum
322\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhaṃ tena kusalena kammunā, catubbhi ṭhānehi visesamajjhagā;
::

::gathalast
Āyuñca {pb:T:0.0047} vaṇṇañca sukhaṃ balañca, khiḍḍāratiṃ paccanubhomanappakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
323\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutaṃ nu taṃ bhāsati yaṃ ayaṃ latā, yaṃ no apucchimha akittayī no;
::

::gathalast
Patino kiramhākaṃ visiṭṭha nārīnaṃ, gatī ca tāsaṃ pavarā ca devatā.
::

::hangnum
324\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patīsu {pb:M:0.0039} dhammaṃ pacarāma sabbā, patibbatā yattha bhavanti itthiyo;
::

::gathalast
Patīsu dhammaṃ pacaritva {note:pacaritvāna (ka.)} sabbā, lacchāmase bhāsati yaṃ ayaṃ latā.
::

::hangnum
325\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīho yathā pabbatasānugocaro, mahindharaṃ pabbatamāvasitvā;
::

::gathalast
Pasayha hantvā itare catuppade, khudde mige khādati maṃsabhojano.
::

::hangnum
326\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva saddhā idha ariyasāvikā, bhattāraṃ nissāya patiṃ anubbatā;
::

::gathalast
Kodhaṃ vadhitvā abhibhuyya maccharaṃ, saggamhi sā modati dhammacārinī’’ti.
::

::centre
Latāvimānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Guttilavimānaṃ

::centre
1. Vatthuttamadāyikāvimānavatthu
::

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattatantiṃ {pb:P:0.0042} sumadhuraṃ, rāmaṇeyyaṃ avācayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:T:0.0048} maṃ raṅgamhi avheti, ‘saraṇaṃ me hohi kosiyā’ti.
::

::hangnum
328\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:V:0.0030} te saraṇaṃ homi, ahamācariyapūjako;
::

::gathalast
Na taṃ jayissati sisso, sissamācariya jessasī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
329\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
::

::gathalast
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
::

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
331\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:M:0.0040} taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vatthuttamadāyikā nārī, pavarā hoti naresu nārīsu;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ piyarūpadāyikā manāpaṃ, dibbaṃ sā labhate upecca ṭhānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā {pb:P:0.0043} me passa vimānaṃ, accharā kāmavaṇṇinīhamasmi;
::

::gathalast
Accharāsahassassāhaṃ, pavarā {note:accharāsahassassāhaṃ pavarā, (syā.)} passa {pb:T:0.0049} puññānaṃ vipākaṃ.
::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

(Anantaraṃ caturavimānaṃ yathā vatthudāyikāvimānaṃ tathā vitthāretabbaṃ {note:( ) natthi sī. potthake})

::hangnum
613\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkhalikaṃ {note:sakkhaliṃ (sī. syā.)} ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
::

::hangnum
614\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā me passa vimānaṃ, accharā kāmavaṇṇinīhamasmi;
::

::gathalast
Accharāsahassassāhaṃ, pavarā passa puññānaṃ vipākaṃ.
::

::hangnum
615\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:V:0.0037} metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
617\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me ajja, suppabhātaṃ suhuṭṭhitaṃ {note:suvuṭṭhitaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ addasāmi {note:addasaṃ (sī. syā.), addasāsiṃ (pī.)} devatāyo, accharā kāmavaṇṇiniyo {note:kāmavaṇṇiyo (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
618\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāsāhaṃ {pb:M:0.0048} {note:tāsāhaṃ (syā. ka.)} dhammaṃ sutvā {note:sutvāna (syā. ka.)}, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ.
::

::gatha2
Dānena samacariyāya, saññamena damena ca;
::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ tattha gamissāmi {note:tattheva gacchāmi (ka.)}, yattha gantvā na socare’’ti.
::

::centre
Guttilavimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Daddallavimānavatthu

::hangnum
619\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daddallamānā {pb:T:0.0059}{pb:P:0.0048} {note:daddaḷhamānā (ka.)} vaṇṇena, yasasā ca yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe deve tāvatiṃse, vaṇṇena atirocasi.
::

::hangnum
620\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dassanaṃ nābhijānāmi, idaṃ paṭhamadassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā kāyā nu āgamma, nāmena bhāsase mama’’nti.
::

::hangnum
621\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ bhadde subhaddāsiṃ, pubbe mānusake bhave;
::

::gathalast
Sahabhariyā ca te āsiṃ, bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā.
::

::hangnum
622\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā ahaṃ kāyassa bhedā, vippamuttā tato cutā;
::

::gathalast
Nimmānaratīnaṃ devānaṃ, upapannā sahabyata’’nti.
::

::hangnum
623\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahūtakatakalyāṇā, te deve yanti pāṇino;
::

::gathalast
Yesaṃ tvaṃ kittayissasi, subhadde jātimattano.
::

::hangnum
624\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha {note:kathaṃ (sī. syā.)} tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena, kena vā anusāsitā;
::

::gathalast
Kīdiseneva dānena, subbatena yasassinī.
::

::hangnum
625\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yasaṃ etādisaṃ pattā, visesaṃ vipulamajjhagā;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
626\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭheva piṇḍapātāni, yaṃ dānaṃ adadaṃ pure;
::

::gathalast
Dakkhiṇeyyassa saṅghassa, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
627\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
629\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:M:0.0049} tayā bahutare bhikkhū, saññate brahmacārayo {note:brahmacarino (syā.), brahmacāriye (pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tappesiṃ annapānena, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
630\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tayā {pb:T:0.0060}{pb:V:0.0038} bahutaraṃ datvā, hīnakāyūpagā ahaṃ {note:ahuṃ (ka. sī.)};
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃ tvaṃ appataraṃ datvā, visesaṃ vipulamajjhagā;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
631\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manobhāvanīyo {pb:P:0.0049} bhikkhu, sandiṭṭho me pure ahu;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ bhattena {note:bhadde (ka.)} nimantesiṃ, revataṃ attanaṭṭhamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
632\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So me atthapurekkhāro, anukampāya revato;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghe dehīti maṃvoca, tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ kariṃ.
::

::hangnum
633\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā, appameyye patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Puggalesu tayā dinnaṃ, na taṃ tava mahapphala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
634\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idānevāhaṃ jānāmi, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sāhaṃ gantvā manussattaṃ, vadaññū vītamaccharā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghe dānāni dassāmi {note:saṅghe dānaṃ dassāmihaṃ (syā.)}, appamattā punappuna’’nti.
::

::hangnum
635\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā esā devatā bhadde, tayā mantayate saha;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe deve tāvatiṃse, vaṇṇena atirocatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
636\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manussabhūtā devinda, pubbe mānusake bhave;
::

::gatha2
Sahabhariyā ca me āsi, bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghe dānāni datvāna, katapuññā virocatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
637\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammena pubbe bhaginī, tayā bhadde virocati;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ saṅghamhi appameyye, patiṭṭhāpesi dakkhiṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
638\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchito hi mayā buddho, gijjhakūṭamhi pabbate;
::

::gathalast
Vipākaṃ {pb:T:0.0061} saṃvibhāgassa, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
639\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
640\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:0.0050} me buddho viyākāsi, jānaṃ kammaphalaṃ sakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vipākaṃ saṃvibhāgassa, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
641\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 750; kathā. 798} ‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito.
::

::hangnum
642\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 751; kathā. 798} ‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
643\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 752; kathā. 798} ‘‘Eso {pb:V:0.0039} hi saṅgho vipulo mahaggato, esappameyyo udadhīva sāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Ete hi seṭṭhā naravīrasāvakā, pabhaṅkarā dhammamudīrayanti {note:dhammakathaṃ udīrayanti (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
644\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 753; kathā. 798} ‘‘Tesaṃ {pb:P:0.0050} sudinnaṃ suhutaṃ suyiṭṭhaṃ, ye saṅghamuddissa dadanti dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā patiṭṭhitā, mahapphalā lokavidūna {note:lokavidūhi (syā. ka.)} vaṇṇitā.
::

::hangnum
645\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 754; kathā. 798} ‘‘Etādisaṃ yaññamanussarantā {note:puññamanussarantā (syā. ka.)}, ye vedajātā vicaranti loke;
::

::gathalast
Vineyya maccheramalaṃ samūlaṃ, aninditā {pb:T:0.0062} saggamupenti ṭhāna’’nti.
::

::centre
Daddallavimānaṃ {note:daddaḷhavimānaṃ (ka.)} chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Pesavatīvimānavatthu

::hangnum
646\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phalikarajatahemajālachannaṃ{pb:P:0.0051}, vividhacitratalamaddasaṃ surammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Byamhaṃ sunimmitaṃ toraṇūpapannaṃ, rucakupakiṇṇamidaṃ subhaṃ vimānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
647\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhāti {pb:M:0.0051} ca dasa disā nabheva suriyo, sarade tamonudo sahassaraṃsī;
::

::gathalast
Tathā tapatimidaṃ tava vimānaṃ, jalamiva dhūmasikho nise nabhagge.
::

::hangnum
648\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Musatīva nayanaṃ sateratāva {note:sateritāva (syā. ka.)}, ākāse ṭhapitamidaṃ manuññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīṇāmurajasammatāḷaghuṭṭhaṃ, iddhaṃ indapuraṃ yathā tavedaṃ.
::

::hangnum
649\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumakumuduppalakuvalayaṃ, yodhika {note:yūdhika (sī.)} bandhukanojakā {note:yothikā bhaṇḍikā nojakā (syā.)} ca santi;
::

::gathalast
Sālakusumitapupphitā asokā, vividhadumaggasugandhasevitamidaṃ.
::

::hangnum
650\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saḷalalabujabhujaka {note:sujaka (sī. syā.)} saṃyuttā {note:saññatā (sī.)}, kusakasuphullitalatāvalambinīhi{pb:T:0.0063};
::

::gathalast
Maṇijālasadisā yasassinī, rammā pokkharaṇī upaṭṭhitā te.
::

::hangnum
651\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Udakaruhā ca yetthi pupphajātā, thalajā ye ca santi rukkhajātā;
::

::gathalast
Mānusakāmānussakā ca dibbā, sabbe tuyhaṃ nivesanamhi jātā.
::

::hangnum
652\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kissa saṃyamadamassayaṃ vipāko, kenāsi kammaphalenidhūpapannā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā ca te adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, tadanupadaṃ avacāsiḷārapamhe’’ti {note:pakhumeti (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
653\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:M:0.0052} ca me adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, koñcamayūracakora {note:caṅkora (ka.)} saṅghacaritaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dibya {note:dibba (sī. pī.)} pilavahaṃsarājaciṇṇaṃ, dijakāraṇḍavakokilābhinaditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
654\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānāsantānakapuppharukkhavividhā, pāṭalijambuasokarukkhavantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathā ca me adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, taṃ {pb:T:0.0064} te pavedayāmi {note:pavadissāmi (sī.), pavedissāmi (pī.)} suṇohi bhante.
::

::hangnum
655\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Magadhavarapuratthimena{pb:P:0.0052}, nāḷakagāmo nāma atthi bhante;
::

::gathalast
Tattha ahosiṃ pure suṇisā, pesavatīti {note:sesavatīti (sī. syā.)} tattha jāniṃsu mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
656\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhamapacitatthadhammakusalaṃ{pb:V:0.0040}, devamanussapūjitaṃ mahantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upatissaṃ nibbutamappameyyaṃ, muditamanā kusumehi abbhukiriṃ {note:abbhokiriṃ (sī. syā. pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
657\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paramagatigatañca pūjayitvā, antimadehadharaṃ isiṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mānusakaṃ samussayaṃ, tidasagatā idha māvasāmi ṭhāna’’nti.
::

::centre
Pesavatīvimānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Mallikāvimānavatthu

::hangnum
658\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pītavatthe {pb:P:0.0053} pītadhaje, pītālaṅkārabhūsite;
::

::gathalast
Pītantarāhi vaggūhi, apiḷandhāva sobhasi.
::

::hangnum
659\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā {pb:M:0.0053} kambukāyūradhare {note:kakambukāyuradhare (syā.)}, kañcanāveḷabhūsite;
::

::gathalast
Hemajālakasañchanne {note:pacchanne (sī.)}, nānāratanamālinī.
::

::hangnum
660\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayā lohitaṅgamayā {note:lohitaṅkamayā (sī. syā.)} ca, muttāmayā {pb:T:0.0065} veḷuriyamayā ca;
::

::gathalast
Masāragallā sahalohitaṅgā {note:sahalohitaṅkā (sī.), sahalohitakā (syā.)}, pārevatakkhīhi maṇīhi cittatā.
::

::hangnum
661\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koci koci ettha mayūrasussaro, haṃsassa rañño karavīkasussaro;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ saro suyyati vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ tūriyamivappavāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
662\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratho ca te subho vaggu {note:vaggū (syā.)}, nānāratanacittito {note:nānāratanacittaṅgo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Nānāvaṇṇāhi dhātūhi, suvibhattova sobhati.
::

::hangnum
663\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ rathe kañcanabimbavaṇṇe, yā tvaṃ {note:yattha (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} ṭhitā bhāsasi maṃ padesaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
664\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇajālaṃ maṇisoṇṇacittitaṃ {note:vicittaṃ (ka.), cittaṃ (sī. syā.)}, muttācitaṃ hemajālena channaṃ {note:sañchannaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Parinibbute gotame appameyye, pasannacittā ahamābhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
665\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna, kusalaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apetasokā sukhitā, sampamodāmanāmayā’’ti.
::

::centre
Mallikāvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 9. Visālakkhivimānavatthu

::hangnum
666\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā {pb:T:0.0066}{pb:M:0.0054}{pb:P:0.0054} nāma tvaṃ visālakkhi {note:visālakkhī (syā.)}, ramme cittalatāvane;
::

::gathalast
Samantā anupariyāsi, nārīgaṇapurakkhatā {note:purakkhitā (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
667\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā {pb:V:0.0041} devā tāvatiṃsā, pavisanti imaṃ vanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sayoggā sarathā sabbe, citrā honti idhāgatā.
::

::hangnum
668\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyhañca idha pattāya, uyyāne vicarantiyā;
::

::gatha2
Kāye na dissatī cittaṃ, kena rūpaṃ tavedisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
669\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena kammena devinda, rūpaṃ mayhaṃ gatī ca me;
::

::gathalast
Iddhi ca ānubhāvo ca, taṃ suṇohi purindada.
::

::hangnum
670\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ rājagahe ramme, sunandā nāmupāsikā;
::

::gathalast
Saddhā sīlena sampannā, saṃvibhāgaratā sadā.
::

::hangnum
671\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Acchādanañca bhattañca, senāsanaṃ padīpiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::hangnum
672\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ {note:catuddasiṃ (pī. ka.)} pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
673\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
::

::gathalast
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
674\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
::

::gathalast
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā.
::

::hangnum
675\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
::

::gathalast
Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino.
::

::hangnum
676\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā {pb:T:0.0067}{pb:P:0.0055} me ñātikulā dāsī {note:ñātikulaṃ āsī (syā. ka.)}, sadā mālābhihārati;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ bhagavato thūpe, sabbamevābhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
677\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uposathe cahaṃ gantvā, mālāgandhavilepanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thūpasmiṃ abhiropesiṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
678\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:0.0055} kammena devinda, rūpaṃ mayhaṃ gatī ca me;
::

::gathalast
Iddhī ca ānubhāvo ca, yaṃ mālaṃ abhiropayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
679\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañca sīlavatī āsiṃ, na taṃ tāva vipaccati;
::

::gathalast
Āsā ca pana me devinda, sakadāgāminī siya’’nti.
::

::centre
Visālakkhivimānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Pāricchattakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
680\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāricchattake {pb:V:0.0042} koviḷāre, ramaṇīye manorame;
::

::gathalast
Dibbamālaṃ ganthamānā, gāyantī sampamodasi.
::

::hangnum
681\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā saddā niccharanti, savanīyā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
682\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā gandhā pavāyanti, sucigandhā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
683\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vivattamānā kāyena, yā veṇīsu piḷandhanā.
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, tūriye pañcaṅgike yathā.
::

::hangnum
684\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakā vātadhutā {note:vātadhūtā (sī. syā.)}, vātena sampakampitā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, tūriye pañcaṅgike yathā.
::

::hangnum
685\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāpi {pb:P:0.0056} te sirasmiṃ mālā, sucigandhā manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Vāti {pb:T:0.0068} gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
::

::hangnum
686\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ghāyase taṃ sucigandhaṃ {note:suciṃ gandhaṃ (sī.)}, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ {note:mānusaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
687\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhassaraṃ accimantaṃ, vaṇṇagandhena saṃyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asokapupphamālāhaṃ, buddhassa upanāmayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
688\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna, kusalaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apetasokā sukhitā, sampamodāmanāmayā’’ti.
::

::centre
Pāricchattakavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Pāricchattakavaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:M:0.0056} –

::gatha1
Uḷāro ucchu pallaṅko, latā ca guttilena ca;
::

::gatha2
Daddallapesamallikā, visālakkhi pāricchattako;
::

::gathalast
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
::

#### 4. Mañjiṭṭhakavaggo

#### 1. Mañjiṭṭhakavimānavatthu

689\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Pañcaṅgike turiyena {note:turiyena (sī. syā. pī.)}, ramasi suppavādite.
::

::hangnum
690\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamhā vimānā oruyha, nimmitā ratanāmayā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
691\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa yasseva sālassa, mūle tiṭṭhasi devate;
::

::gathalast
So so muñcati pupphāni, onamitvā dumuttamo.
::

::hangnum
692\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vāteritaṃ sālavanaṃ, ādhutaṃ {note:ādhūtaṃ (sī.)} dijasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vāti gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
::

::hangnum
693\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
694\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, dāsī ayirakule {note:ayyirakule (syā. ka.)} ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaṃ nisinnaṃ disvāna, sālapupphehi okiriṃ.
::

::hangnum
695\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakañca sukataṃ, sālapupphamayaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Buddhassa upanāmesiṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
696\.
::

::centre

#### 2. Pabhassaravimānavatthu

::hangnum
697\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhassaravaravaṇṇanibhe{pb:P:0.0058}, surattavatthavasane {note:vatthanivāsane (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Mahiddhike candanaruciragatte, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
698\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pallaṅko {pb:V:0.0044} ca te mahaggho, nānāratanacittito {pb:T:0.0070} ruciro;
::

::gathalast
Yattha tvaṃ nisinnā virocasi, devarājāriva nandane vane.
::

::hangnum
699\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure sucaritamācarī bhadde, kissa kammassa vipākaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Anubhosi devalokasmiṃ, devate pucchitācikkha;
::

::gathalast
Kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
700\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piṇḍāya te carantassa, mālaṃ phāṇitañca adadaṃ bhante;
::

::gathalast
Tassa kammassidaṃ vipākaṃ, anubhomi devalokasmiṃ.
::

::hangnum
701\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hoti ca me anutāpo, aparaddhaṃ {note:aparādhaṃ (syā.)} dukkhitañca {note:dukkaṭañca (sī.)} me bhante;
::

::gathalast
Sāhaṃ dhammaṃ nāssosiṃ, sudesitaṃ dhammarājena.
::

::hangnum
702\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ taṃ vadāmi bhaddante, ‘yassa me anukampiyo koci;
::

::gathalast
Dhammesu taṃ samādapetha’, sudesitaṃ dhammarājena.
::

::hangnum
703\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ atthi saddhā buddhe, dhamme {pb:T:0.0071} ca saṅgharatane;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ ativirocanti, āyunā yasasā siriyā.
::

::hangnum
704\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patāpena vaṇṇena uttaritarā,
::

::gathalast
Aññe mahiddhikatarā mayā devā’’ti;
::

::centre
Pabhassaravimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Nāgavimānavatthu

::hangnum
705\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alaṅkatā {pb:M:0.0058}{pb:P:0.0059} maṇikañcanācitaṃ, sovaṇṇajālacitaṃ mahantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhiruyha gajavaraṃ sukappitaṃ, idhāgamā vehāyasaṃ {note:vehāsayaṃ (sī.)} antalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
706\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgassa dantesu duvesu nimmitā, acchodakā {note:acchodikā (sī. ka.)} paduminiyo suphullā;
::

::gathalast
Padumesu ca turiyagaṇā pabhijjare, imā ca naccanti manoharāyo.
::

::hangnum
707\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
708\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bārāṇasiyaṃ {pb:T:0.0072} upasaṅkamitvā, buddhassahaṃ vatthayugaṃ adāsiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pādāni vanditvā {note:vanditva (sī.)} chamā nisīdiṃ, vittā cahaṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ.
::

::hangnum
709\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho ca me kañcanasannibhattaco, adesayi samudayadukkhaniccataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asaṅkhataṃ dukkhanirodhasassataṃ, maggaṃ adesayi {note:adesesi (sī.)} yato vijānisaṃ;
::

::hangnum
710\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appāyukī {pb:V:0.0045} kālakatā tato cutā, upapannā tidasagaṇaṃ yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Sakkassahaṃ aññatarā pajāpati, yasuttarā nāma disāsu vissutā’’ti.
::

::centre
Nāgavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Alomavimānavatthu

::hangnum
711\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
712\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.

::hangnum
714\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
715\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca {pb:T:0.0073} bārāṇasiyaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
716\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukkhāya aloṇikāya ca, passa phalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā;
::

::gathalast
Alomaṃ sukhitaṃ disvā, ko puññaṃ na karissati.
::

::hangnum
717\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… {pb:P:0.0061} vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Alomavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

725\.

726\.

::gathalast

727\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
728\.

::

::gathalast
Ekassa kañjikadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasi’’nti.

::centre

741\.

::gathalast

742\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
743\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
744\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāyeva te suddhanumodanāya, laddhaṃ vimānabbhutadassaneyyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yā ceva sā dānamadāsi nārī, tassā gatiṃ brūhi kuhiṃ uppannā {note:upapannā (ka.)} sā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
745\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā sā ahu mayhaṃ sakhī bhadante, saṅghassa kāresi mahāvihāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Viññātadhammā sā adāsi dānaṃ, uppannā nimmānaratīsu devesu.
::

::hangnum
746\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pajāpatī {pb:M:0.0062} tassa sunimmitassa, acintiyā kammavipākā tassa;
::

::gathalast
Yametaṃ pucchasi kuhiṃ uppannā {note:upapannā (ka.)} sāti, taṃ te viyākāsiṃ anaññathā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
747\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tenahaññepi samādapetha, saṅghassa dānāni dadātha vittā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammañca suṇātha pasannamānasā, sudullabho laddho manussalābho.
::

::hangnum
748\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:T:0.0077} maggaṃ maggādhipatī adesayi {note:maggādhipatyadesayi (sī.)}, brahmassaro kañcanasannibhattaco;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghassa dānāni dadātha vittā, mahapphalā yattha bhavanti dakkhiṇā.
::

::hangnum
749\.
::

::gatha1
{note:khu. pā. 6.6; su. ni. 229} ‘‘Ye {pb:P:0.0064} puggalā aṭṭha sataṃ pasatthā, cattāri etāni yugāni honti;
::

::gathalast
Te dakkhiṇeyyā sugatassa sāvakā, etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni.
::

::hangnum
750\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 641} ‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito.
::

::hangnum
751\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 642} ‘‘Yajamānānaṃ {pb:V:0.0048} manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
752\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 643} ‘‘Eso hi saṅgho vipulo mahaggato, esappameyyo udadhīva sāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Etehi seṭṭhā naravīrasāvakā, pabhaṅkarā dhammamudīrayanti {note:natthettha pāṭhabhedo}.
::

::hangnum
753\.
::

::gatha1
{note:vi. va. 644} ‘‘Tesaṃ sudinnaṃ suhutaṃ suyiṭṭhaṃ, ye saṅghamuddissa dadanti dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā patiṭṭhitā, mahapphalā lokavidūna {note:lokavidūhi (ka.)} vaṇṇitā.
::

::hangnum
754\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etādisaṃ {pb:T:0.0078}{pb:M:0.0063} yaññamanussarantā, ye vedajātā vicaranti loke;
::

::gathalast
Vineyya maccheramalaṃ samūlaṃ, aninditā saggamupenti ṭhāna’’nti.
::

::centre
Vihāravimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

::centre
Bhāṇavāraṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 9. Pītavimānavatthu

::hangnum

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
796\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pītapāsādasayane, pītāsane pītabhājane;
::

::gathalast
Pītachatte pītarathe, pītasse pītabījane.
::

::hangnum
797\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ {pb:T:0.0082}{pb:M:0.0066} kammamakarī bhadde, pubbe mānusake bhave;

::gathalast

::hangnum
798\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kosātakī nāma latatthi bhante, tittikā anabhicchitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
799\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satthu sarīramuddissa, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Nāssa maggaṃ avekkhissaṃ, na taggamanasā {note:tadaggamanasā (sī.), tadaṅgamanasā (syā.)} satī.
::

::hangnum
800\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato maṃ avadhī gāvī, thūpaṃ apattamānasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tañcāhaṃ abhisañceyyaṃ, bhiyyo {note:bhīyo (sī. aṭṭha.)} nūna ito siyā.
::

::hangnum
801\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena kammena devinda, maghavā devakuñjaro;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tava sahabya {note:sahabyata (sī. syā.)} māgatā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
802\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ {pb:P:0.0069} sutvā tidasādhipati, maghavā devakuñjaro;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
803\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
804\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
805\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
806\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

#### 10. Ucchuvimānavatthu

::hangnum
808\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Siriyā ca vaṇṇena yasena tejasā, brahmāva deve tidase sahindake.
::

::hangnum
809\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:P:0.0070} taṃ uppalamāladhārinī, āveḷinī kañcanasannibhattace;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkate uttamavatthadhārinī, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
810\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūtā purimāya jātiyā;
::

::gatha2
Dānaṃ suciṇṇaṃ atha sīlasaññamaṃ, kenupapannā sugatiṃ yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
811\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idāni bhante imameva gāmaṃ, piṇḍāya amhāka gharaṃ upāgami;
::

::gathalast
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā;
::

::hangnum
812\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sassu {pb:T:0.0084} ca pacchā anuyuñjate mamaṃ, kahaṃ nu ucchuṃ vadhuke avākirī;
::

::gathalast
Na chaḍḍitaṃ no pana khāditaṃ mayā, santassa bhikkhussa sayaṃ adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
813\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyhaṃnvidaṃ issariyaṃ atho mama, itissā sassu paribhāsate mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Leḍḍuṃ gahetvā pahāraṃ adāsi me, tato cutā kālakatāmhi devatā.
::

::hangnum
814\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
::

::hangnum
815\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva {pb:M:0.0068} kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
816\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
817\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
818\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvañca {pb:P:0.0071} bhante anukampakaṃ viduṃ, upecca vandiṃ kusalañca pucchisaṃ;

::gathalast
Tato te ucchussa adāsiṃ khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā’’ti.

::centre

828\.

::gatha1

829\.

830\.

831\.

::hangnum
832\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ghāyase {pb:P:0.0073} taṃ sucigandhaṃ, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ;

::gathalast

::hangnum
833\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dāsī {pb:V:0.0053} ahaṃ pure āsiṃ, gayāyaṃ brāhmaṇassahaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
834\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkosānaṃ vadhānañca, tajjanāya ca uggatā {note:ukkatā (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Kuṭaṃ {pb:T:0.0087} gahetvā nikkhamma, agañchiṃ {note:āgacchiṃ (syā. ka.), agacchiṃ (pī.), gacchiṃ (sī.)} udahāriyā {note:udakahāriyā (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
835\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vipathe {pb:M:0.0070} kuṭaṃ nikkhipitvā, vanasaṇḍaṃ upāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idhevāhaṃ marissāmi, ko attho {note:kvatthosi (ka.), kīvatthopi (syā.)} jīvitena me.
::

::hangnum
836\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daḷhaṃ pāsaṃ karitvāna, āsumbhitvāna pādape;
::

::gathalast
Tato disā vilokesiṃ,ko nu kho vanamassito.
::

::hangnum
837\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, sabbalokahitaṃ muniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisinnaṃ rukkhamūlasmiṃ, jhāyantaṃ akutobhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
838\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā me ahu saṃvego, abbhuto lomahaṃsano;
::

::gathalast
Ko nu kho vanamassito, manusso udāhu devatā.
::

::hangnum
839\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāsādikaṃ pasādanīyaṃ, vanā nibbanamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvā mano me pasīdi, nāyaṃ yādisakīdiso.
::

::hangnum
840\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Guttindriyo jhānarato, abahiggatamānaso;
::

::gathalast
Hito sabbassa lokassa, buddho ayaṃ {note:soyaṃ (sī.)} bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
841\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhayabheravo durāsado, sīhova guhamassito;
::

::gathalast
Dullabhāyaṃ dassanāya, pupphaṃ odumbaraṃ yathā.
::

::hangnum
842\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So maṃ mudūhi vācāhi, ālapitvā tathāgato;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
843\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ giraṃ suṇitvāna, nelaṃ atthavatiṃ suciṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
844\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kallacittañca maṃ ñatvā, pasannaṃ suddhamānasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hito {pb:T:0.0088} sabbassa lokassa, anusāsi tathāgato.
::

::hangnum
845\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ dukkhanti maṃvoca, ayaṃ dukkhassa sambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Dukkha {note:ayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} nirodho maggo ca {note:dukkhanirodho ca (syā.)}, añjaso amatogadho.
::

::hangnum
846\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anukampakassa {pb:M:0.0071} kusalassa, ovādamhi ahaṃ ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhagā amataṃ santiṃ, nibbānaṃ padamaccutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
847\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhaṃ avaṭṭhitāpemā, dassane avikampinī;
::

::gathalast
Mūlajātāya saddhāya, dhītā buddhassa orasā.
::

::hangnum
848\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhaṃ {pb:V:0.0054}{pb:P:0.0074} ramāmi kīḷāmi, modāmi akutobhayā;
::

::gathalast
Dibbamālaṃ dhārayāmi, pivāmi madhumaddavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
849\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni, paṭibodhaṃ karonti me;
::

::gathalast
Āḷambo gaggaro bhīmo, sādhuvādī ca saṃsayo.
::

::hangnum
850\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pokkharo ca suphasso ca, vīṇāmokkhā ca nāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Nandā ceva sunandā ca, soṇadinnā sucimhitā.
::

::hangnum
851\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alambusā missakesī ca, puṇḍarīkātidāruṇī {note:… ticāruṇī (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Eṇīphassā suphassā {note:supassā (syā. pī. ka.)} ca, subhaddā {note:saṃbhaddā (ka.)} muduvādinī.
::

::hangnum
852\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etā caññā ca seyyāse, accharānaṃ pabodhikā;
::

::gathalast
Tā maṃ kālenupāgantvā, abhibhāsanti devatā.
::

::hangnum
853\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Handa naccāma gāyāma, handa taṃ ramayāmase;
::

::gathalast
Nayidaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, katapuññānamevidaṃ.
::

::hangnum
854\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asokaṃ {pb:T:0.0089} nandanaṃ rammaṃ, tidasānaṃ mahāvanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, idha natthi parattha ca.
::

::hangnum
855\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhañca katapuññānaṃ, idha ceva parattha ca;
::

::gatha2
Tesaṃ sahabyakāmānaṃ, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katapuññā hi modanti, sagge bhogasamaṅgino.
::

::hangnum
856\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūnaṃ vata atthāya, uppajjanti tathāgatā;
::

::gatha2
Dakkhiṇeyyā manussānaṃ, puññakhettānamākarā;
::

::gathalast
Yattha kāraṃ karitvāna, sagge modanti dāyakā’’ti.
::

::centre
Rajjumālāvimānaṃ dvādasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Mañjiṭṭhakavaggo catuttho niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:P:0.0076} –

::gatha1
Mañjiṭṭhā {pb:M:0.0072} pabhassarā nāgā, alomākañjikadāyikā;
::

::gatha2
Vihāracaturitthambā, pītā ucchuvandanarajjumālā ca;
::

::gathalast
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
::

::centre
Itthivimānaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 2. Purisavimānaṃ

#### 5. Mahārathavaggo

#### 1. Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānavatthu

::hangnum
857\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:M:0.0073}{pb:V:0.0055}{pb:P:0.0077} me vandati pādāni, iddhiyā yasasā jalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, sabbā obhāsayaṃ disā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
858\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇḍūkohaṃ pure āsiṃ, udake vārigocaro;
::

::gathalast
Tava dhammaṃ suṇantassa, avadhī vacchapālako.
::

::hangnum
859\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Muhuttaṃ {pb:T:0.0090} cittapasādassa, iddhiṃ passa yasañca me;
::

::gathalast
Ānubhāvañca me passa, vaṇṇaṃ passa jutiñca me.
::

::hangnum
860\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca te dīghamaddhānaṃ, dhammaṃ assosuṃ gotama;
::

::gathalast
Pattā te acalaṭṭhānaṃ, yattha gantvā na socare’’ti.
::

::centre
Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Revatīvimānavatthu

::hangnum

::hangnum
862\.

::hangnum
863\.

{note:pe. va. 714}‘‘Uṭṭhehi revate supāpadhamme, apārutadvāre {note:apārubhaṃ dvāraṃ (sī. syā.), apārutadvāraṃ (pī. ka.)} adānasīle;

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gathalast
Taṃ dissati sūriyasamānavaṇṇaṃ, so modati saggapatto vimāne’’ti.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
870\.

::hangnum

::hangnum
872\.

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gathalast

#### 3. Chattamāṇavakavimānavatthu

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Pāragato balavīriyasamaṅgī {note:balavīrasamaṅgī (ka.)}, taṃ sugataṃ saraṇatthamupehi.

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgavirāgamanejamasokaṃ, dhammamasaṅkhatamappaṭikūlaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
888\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha {pb:P:0.0081} ca dinna mahapphalamāhu, catūsu sucīsu purisayugesu;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
889\.

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0077} tathā tapati nabhe sūriyo, cando ca na bhāsati na phusso;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
890\.

::hangnum
891\.

‘‘Bahupadumavicitrapuṇḍarīkaṃ, vokiṇṇaṃ kusumehi nekacittaṃ;

::hangnum
892\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
893\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naranāriyo {note:naranārī (ka.), nāriyo (?)} bahuketthanekavaṇṇā, kusumavibhūsitābharaṇettha sumanā;

::gathalast
Anilapamuñcitā pavanti {note:pavāyanti (ka.)} surabhiṃ, tapaniyavitatā suvaṇṇachannā {note:suvaṇṇacchādanā (sī.)}.

::hangnum

::gathalast

895\.

896\.

::

::gathalast

897\.

::gatha3

903\.

::gathalast
Tena sucaritena kammunāhaṃ {note:kammanāhaṃ (sī.)}, uppanno {note:upapanno (bahūsu)} tidivesu kāmakāmī.

::hangnum
904\.

::gatha1

::

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
906\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
907\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
908\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ upagatomhi saccanāmaṃ, anukampassu punapi suṇemu {note:suṇoma (sī.), suṇomi (syā.)} dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
909\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:0.0080} cidha {note:yedha (sī. syā. pī.), ye idha (ka.)} pajahanti kāmarāgaṃ, bhavarāgānusayañca pahāya mohaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::centre

#### 4. Kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
910\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccamidaṃ {pb:T:0.0099}{pb:P:0.0084} maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā {note:ruciratthatā (syā. ka.) 646 gāthāyaṃ ‘‘rucakupakiṇṇaṃ’’ti padassa saṃvaṇṇanā passitabbā} subhā.
::

::hangnum
911\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthacchasi {pb:P:0.0085} pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ {note:vaggu (sī. ka.), vaggū (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
::

::hangnum
912\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
913\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ deva mahānubhāva, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
914\.
::

::gatha1
So devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
915\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satisamuppādakaro{pb:V:0.0060}, dvāre kakkaṭako ṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Niṭṭhito jātarūpassa, sobhati dasapādako.
::

::hangnum
916\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:0.0081} metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti {pb:T:0.0100} ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
917\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūto yamakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

(Anantaraṃ pañcavimānaṃ yathā kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānaṃ tathā vitthāretabbaṃ)

#### 5. Dvārapālavimānavatthu

::hangnum
918\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccamidaṃ {pb:P:0.0086} maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
::

::hangnum
919\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
::

::hangnum
920\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… {pb:T:0.0101} vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
922\.
::

::gatha1
So devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
923\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbaṃ mamaṃ vassasahassamāyu, vācābhigītaṃ manasā pavattitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ettāvatā ṭhassati puññakammo, dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto.
::

::hangnum
924\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:0.0082} metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Dvārapālavimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Paṭhamanāgavimānavatthu

961\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Abhiruyha gajavaraṃ {note:gajaṃ varaṃ (syā.)} sukappitaṃ, idhāgamā vehāyasaṃ antalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
962\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgassa dantesu duvesu nimmitā, acchodakā paduminiyo suphullā;
::

::gathalast

963\.

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gathalast

#### 12. Tatiyanāgavimānavatthu

::hangnum
976\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:V:0.0064}{pb:P:0.0090} nu dibbena yānena, sabbasetena hatthinā;
::

::gathalast
Turiyatāḷitanigghoso, antalikkhe mahīyati.
::

::hangnum
977\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu {note:ādu (sī. syā.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Ajānantā taṃ pucchāma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::hangnum
978\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namhi {pb:M:0.0087} devo na gandhabbo, nāpi {note:nāmhi (ka.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Sudhammā nāma ye devā, tesaṃ aññataro aha’’nti.
::

::hangnum
979\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāma devaṃ sudhammaṃ {note:deva sudhamma (syā.), deva sudhammaṃ (ka.)}, puthuṃ katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ katvā mānuse kammaṃ, sudhammaṃ upapajjatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
980\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ucchāgāraṃ tiṇāgāraṃ, vatthāgārañca yo dade;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇṇaṃ aññataraṃ datvā, sudhammaṃ upapajjatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Tatiyanāgavimānaṃ dvādasamaṃ.
::

#### 13. Cūḷarathavimānavatthu

::hangnum
981\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daḷhadhammā nisārassa, dhanuṃ olubbha tiṭṭhasi;
::

::gathalast
Khattiyo nusi rājañño, adu luddo vanecaro’’ti {note:vanācaroti (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
982\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assakādhipatissāhaṃ{pb:T:0.0106}, bhante putto vanecaro;
::

::gathalast
Nāmaṃ me bhikkhu te brūmi, sujāto iti maṃ vidū {note:viduṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
983\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mige gavesamānohaṃ, ogāhanto brahāvanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Migaṃ tañceva {note:migaṃ gantveva (syā.), migavadhañca (ka.)} nāddakkhiṃ, tañca disvā ṭhito aha’’nti.
::

::hangnum
984\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:P:0.0091} te mahāpuñña, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etto udakamādāya, pāde pakkhālayassu te.
::

::hangnum
985\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ, ābhataṃ girigabbharā;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputta tato pitvā {note:pītvā (sī. syā.)}, santhatasmiṃ upāvisā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
986\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kalyāṇī vata te vācā, savanīyā mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Nelā atthavatī {note:catthavatī (sī.)} vaggu, mantvā {note:mantā (syā. pī. ka.)} atthañca bhāsasi {note:bhāsase (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
987\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā {pb:V:0.0065} te rati vane viharato, isinisabha vadehi puṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Tava vacanapathaṃ nisāmayitvā, atthadhammapadaṃ samācaremase’’ti.
::

::hangnum
988\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahiṃsā {pb:M:0.0088} sabbapāṇīnaṃ, kumāramhāka ruccati;
::

::gathalast
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārati.
::

::hangnum
989\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārati samacariyā ca, bāhusaccaṃ kataññutā;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭheva dhamme pāsaṃsā, dhammā ete pasaṃsiyāti.
::

::hangnum
990\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santike maraṇaṃ tuyhaṃ, oraṃ māsehi pañcahi;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputta {pb:T:0.0107} vijānāhi, attānaṃ parimocayā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
991\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katamaṃ svāhaṃ janapadaṃ gantvā, kiṃ kammaṃ kiñca porisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāya vā pana vijjāya, bhaveyyaṃ ajarāmaro’’ti.
::

::hangnum
992\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na vijjate so padeso, kammaṃ vijjā ca porisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yattha gantvā bhave macco, rājaputtājarāmaro.
::

::hangnum
993\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahaddhanā mahābhogā, raṭṭhavantopi khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtadhanadhaññāse, tepi no {note:tepi na (bahūsu)} ajarāmarā.
::

::hangnum
994\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi te sutā andhakaveṇḍuputtā {note:andhakaveṇhuputtā (sī.), aṇḍakaveṇḍaputtā (syā. ka.)}, sūrā vīrā vikkantappahārino;
::

::gathalast
Tepi āyukkhayaṃ pattā, viddhastā sassatīsamā.
::

::hangnum
995\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gathalast
Ete caññe ca jātiyā, tepi no ajarāmarā.
::

::hangnum
996\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye mantaṃ parivattenti, chaḷaṅgaṃ brahmacintitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ete caññe ca vijjāya, tepi no ajarāmarā.
::

::hangnum
997\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isayo cāpi ye santā, saññatattā tapassino;
::

::gathalast
Sarīraṃ tepi kālena, vijahanti tapassino.
::

::hangnum
998\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhāvitattāpi {pb:P:0.0092} arahanto, katakiccā anāsavā;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhipanti imaṃ dehaṃ, puññapāpaparikkhayā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
999\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitā atthavatī, gāthāyo te mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Nijjhattomhi {pb:T:0.0108} subhaṭṭhena, tvañca me saraṇaṃ bhavā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1000\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:0.0089} maṃ tvaṃ saraṇaṃ gaccha, tameva saraṇaṃ vaja {note:bhaja (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sakyaputtaṃ mahāvīraṃ, yamahaṃ saraṇaṃ gato’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1001\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katarasmiṃ so janapade, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi daṭṭhuṃ gacchissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggala’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1002\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puratthimasmiṃ {pb:V:0.0066} janapade, okkākakulasambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Tatthāsi purisājañño, so ca kho parinibbuto’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1003\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi buddho tiṭṭheyya, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Yojanāni sahassāni, gaccheyyaṃ {note:gacche (syā. pī. ka.)} payirupāsituṃ.
::

::hangnum
1004\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato ca kho {note:yatā kho (pī. ka.)} parinibbuto, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
::

::gathalast
Nibbutampi {note:parinibbutaṃ (syā. ka.)} mahāvīraṃ, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1005\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upemi saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ, dhammañcāpi anuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghañca naradevassa, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1006\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viramāmi khippaṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayāmi;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapo no ca musā bhaṇāmi, sakena dārena ca homi tuṭṭho’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1007\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassaraṃsīva yathā mahappabho, disaṃ yathā bhāti nabhe anukkamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathāpakāro {note:tathappakāro (sī. syā.)} tavāyaṃ {note:tavayaṃ (sī. pī.)} mahāratho, samantato {pb:T:0.0109} yojanasattamāyato.
::

::hangnum
1008\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇapaṭṭehi samantamotthaṭo, urassa muttāhi maṇīhi cittito;
::

::gathalast
Lekhā suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca, sobhenti veḷuriyamayā sunimmitā.
::

::hangnum
1009\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīsañcidaṃ {pb:M:0.0090} veḷuriyassa nimmitaṃ, yugañcidaṃ lohitakāya cittitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yuttā suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca, sobhanti assā ca ime manojavā.
::

::hangnum
1010\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tiṭṭhasi hemarathe adhiṭṭhito, devānamindova sahassavāhano;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi tāhaṃ yasavanta kovidaṃ {note:kovida (ka.)}, kathaṃ tayā laddho ayaṃ uḷāro’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1011\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sujāto {pb:P:0.0093} nāmahaṃ bhante, rājaputto pure ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca maṃ anukampāya, saññamasmiṃ nivesayi.
::

::hangnum
1012\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khīṇāyukañca maṃ ñatvā, sarīraṃ pādāsi satthuno;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ sujāta pūjehi, taṃ te atthāya hehiti.
::

::hangnum
1013\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ gandhehi mālehi, pūjayitvā samuyyuto;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, upapannomhi nandanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1014\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandane {pb:T:0.0110} ca vane {note:nandanopavane (sī.), nandane pavane (syā. ka.)} ramme, nānādijagaṇāyute;
::

::gathalast
Ramāmi naccagītehi, accharāhi purakkhato’’ti.
::

::centre
Cūḷarathavimānaṃ terasamaṃ.
::

#### 14. Mahārathavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1015\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassayuttaṃ {pb:V:0.0067}{pb:P:0.0094} hayavāhanaṃ subhaṃ, āruyhimaṃ sandanaṃ nekacittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uyyānabhūmiṃ abhito anukkamaṃ, purindado bhūtapatīva vāsavo.
::

::hangnum
1016\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayā te rathakubbarā ubho, phalehi {note:thalehi (sī.)} aṃsehi atīva saṅgatā;
::

::gathalast
Sujātagumbā naravīraniṭṭhitā, virocatī pannaraseva cando.
::

::hangnum
1017\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇajālāvatato {pb:M:0.0091} ratho ayaṃ, bahūhi nānāratanehi cittito;
::

::gathalast
Sunandighoso ca subhassaro ca, virocatī cāmarahatthabāhubhi.
::

::hangnum
1018\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imā ca nābhyo manasābhinimmitā, rathassa pādantaramajjhabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Imā ca nābhyo satarājicittitā, sateratā vijjurivappabhāsare.
::

::hangnum
1019\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anekacittāvatato {pb:T:0.0111} ratho ayaṃ, puthū ca nemī ca sahassaraṃsiko;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ saro suyyati {note:sūyati (sī.)} vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ turiyamivappavāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1020\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sirasmiṃ {pb:P:0.0095} cittaṃ maṇicandakappitaṃ, sadā visuddhaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇarājīhi atīva saṅgataṃ, veḷuriyarājīva atīva sobhati.
::

::hangnum
1021\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime ca vāḷī maṇicandakappitā, ārohakambū sujavā brahūpamā.
::

::gathalast
Brahā mahantā balino mahājavā, mano tavaññāya tatheva siṃsare {note:sabbare (ka.), sappare (?)}.
::

::hangnum
1022\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime ca sabbe sahitā catukkamā, mano tavaññāya tatheva siṃsare;
::

::gathalast
Samaṃ vahantā mudukā anuddhatā, āmodamānā turagāna {note:turaṅgāna (ka.)} muttamā.
::

::hangnum
1023\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhunanti vagganti patanti {note:pavattanti (pī. ka.)} cambare, abbhuddhunantā sukate piḷandhane;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ saro suyyati vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ {pb:T:0.0112} turiyamivappavāditaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1024\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rathassa {pb:M:0.0092} ghoso apiḷandhanāna ca, khurassa nādo {note:nādī (syā.), nādi (pī. ka.)} abhihiṃsanāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Ghoso suvaggū samitassa suyyati, gandhabbatūriyāni vicitrasaṃvane.
::

::hangnum
1025\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rathe ṭhitā tā migamandalocanā, āḷārapamhā hasitā piyaṃvadā;
::

::gathalast
Veḷuriyajālāvatatā tanucchavā, sadeva gandhabbasūraggapūjitā.
::

::hangnum
1026\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā rattarattambarapītavāsasā, visālanettā abhirattalocanā;
::

::gathalast
Kule sujātā sutanū sucimhitā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1027\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā kambukeyūradharā suvāsasā, sumajjhimā ūruthanūpapannā;
::

::gathalast
Vaṭṭaṅguliyo sumukhā sudassanā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1028\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññā suveṇī susu missakesiyo, samaṃ vibhattāhi pabhassarāhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Anubbatā tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1029\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āveḷiniyo {pb:V:0.0068} padumuppalacchadā, alaṅkatā candanasāravāsitā {note:vositā (syā.), bhūsitā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Anubbatā {pb:T:0.0113} tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1030\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā {pb:P:0.0096} māliniyo padumuppalacchadā, alaṅkatā candanasāravāsitā;
::

::gathalast
Anubbatā tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1031\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṇṭhesu {pb:M:0.0093} te yāni piḷandhanāni, hatthesu pādesu tatheva sīse;
::

::gathalast
Obhāsayantī dasa sabbaso disā, abbhuddayaṃ sāradikova bhāṇumā.
::

::hangnum
1032\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vātassa vegena ca sampakampitā, bhujesu mālā apiḷandhanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Muñcanti ghosaṃ rūciraṃ suciṃ subhaṃ, sabbehi viññūhi sutabbarūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1033\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uyyānabhūmyā ca duvaddhato ṭhitā, rathā {pb:T:0.0114} ca nāgā tūriyāni ca saro;
::

::gathalast
Tameva devinda pamodayanti, vīṇā yathā pokkharapattabāhubhi.
::

::hangnum
1034\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāsu vīṇāsu bahūsu vaggūsu, manuññarūpāsu hadayeritaṃ pītiṃ {note:hadayeritaṃ pati (sī.), hadayeritampi taṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Pavajjamānāsu atīva accharā, bhamanti kaññā padumesu sikkhitā.
::

::hangnum
1035\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā ca gītāni ca vāditāni ca, naccāni cimāni {note:cemāni (sī.)} samenti ekato;
::

::gathalast
Athettha naccanti athettha accharā, obhāsayantī ubhato varitthiyo.
::

::hangnum
1036\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So modasi turiyagaṇappabodhano, mahīyamāno vajirāvudhoriva;
::

::gathalast
Imāsu vīṇāsu bahūsu vaggūsu, manuññarūpāsu hadayeritaṃ pītiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1037\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūto purimāya jātiyā;
::

::gathalast
Uposathaṃ kaṃ vā {note:uposathaṃ kiṃ va (syā.)} tuvaṃ upāvasi, kaṃ {note:kiṃ (syā.)} dhammacariyaṃ vatamābhirocayi.
::

::hangnum
1038\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nayīdamappassa {pb:M:0.0094} katassa {note:nayidaṃ appassa katassa (sī. syā.), sāsedaṃ appakatassa (ka.)} kammuno, pubbe suciṇṇassa uposathassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Iddhānubhāvo {pb:T:0.0115} vipulo ayaṃ tava, yaṃ devasaṅghaṃ abhirocase bhusaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1039\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānassa te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
::

::gathalast
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1040\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:P:0.0097} devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalanti.
::

::hangnum
1041\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jitindriyaṃ buddhamanomanikkamaṃ, naruttamaṃ kassapamaggapuggalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avāpurantaṃ amatassa dvāraṃ, devātidevaṃ satapuññalakkhaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1042\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamaddasaṃ kuñjaramoghatiṇṇaṃ, suvaṇṇasiṅgīnadabimbasādisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna taṃ khippamahuṃ sucīmano, tameva disvāna subhāsitaddhajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1043\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamannapānaṃ athavāpi cīvaraṃ, suciṃ paṇītaṃ rasasā upetaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pupphābhikkiṇamhi sake nivesane, patiṭṭhapesiṃ sa asaṅgamānaso.
::

::hangnum
1044\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamannapānena {pb:V:0.0069} ca cīvarena ca, khajjena bhojjena ca sāyanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Santappayitvā {pb:T:0.0116} dvipadānamuttamaṃ, so saggaso devapure ramāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1045\.
::



‘‘Etenupāyena imaṃ niraggaḷaṃ, yaññaṃ yajitvā tividhaṃ visuddhaṃ.

::gathalast
Pahāyahaṃ mānusakaṃ samussayaṃ, indūpamo {note:indassamo (syā. ka.)} devapure ramāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1046\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āyuñca {pb:M:0.0095} vaṇṇañca sukhaṃ balañca, paṇītarūpaṃ abhikaṅkhatā muni;
::

::gathalast
Annañca pānañca bahuṃ susaṅkhataṃ, patiṭṭhapetabbamasaṅgamānase.
::

::hangnum
1047\.
::

::gatha1
{note:kathā. 799}‘‘Nayimasmiṃ loke parasmiṃ {note:nayimasmiṃ vā loke parasmiṃ (kathāvatthu 799), nayimasmi loke va parasmi (?)} vā pana, buddhena seṭṭho va samo va vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Āhuneyyānaṃ {note:yamāhuneyyānaṃ (ka.)} paramāhutiṃ gato, puññatthikānaṃ vipulapphalesina’’nti.
::

::centre
Mahārathavimānaṃ cuddasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Mahārathavaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:P:0.0100} –

::gatha1
Maṇḍūko revatī chatto, kakkaṭo dvārapālako;
::

::gatha2
Dve karaṇīyā dve sūci, tayo nāgā ca dve rathā;
::

::gathalast
Purisānaṃ paṭhamo vaggo pavuccatīti.
::

::centre
Bhāṇavāraṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

#### 6. Pāyāsivaggo

#### 1. Paṭhamaagāriyavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1048\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:T:0.0117}{pb:V:0.0070}{pb:P:0.0101} vanaṃ cittalataṃ pabhāsati {note:pakāsati (ka.)}, uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ tidasānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ tuyhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
1049\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1050\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:M:0.0096} devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1051\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca bhariyā ca manussaloke, opānabhūtā gharamāvasimha;
::

::gathalast
Annañca pānañca pasannacittā, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adamha.
::

::hangnum
1052\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamaagāriyavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 3. Phaladāyakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1060\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccamidaṃ {pb:V:0.0071}{pb:M:0.0097}{pb:P:0.0103} maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato soḷasa yojanāni;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
::

::hangnum
1061\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā {pb:T:0.0119} ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
::

::gatha2
Aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā, dibbā ca kaññā tidasacarā uḷārā;
::

::gathalast
Naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
::

::hangnum
1062\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1063\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
1064\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phaladāyī phalaṃ vipulaṃ labhati, dadamujugatesu pasannamānaso;
::

::gathalast
So hi pamodati {note:modati (sī. syā. pī.)} saggagato tidive {note:tattha (ka.)}, anubhoti ca puññaphalaṃ vipulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1065\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tavevāhaṃ {note:tathevāhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} mahāmuni, adāsiṃ caturo phale.
::

::hangnum
1066\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi phalaṃ alameva dātuṃ, niccaṃ manussena sukhatthikena;
::

::gathalast
Dibbāni vā patthayatā sukhāni, manussasobhaggatamicchatā vā.
::

::hangnum
1067\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:T:0.0120} metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Phaladāyakavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 7. Yavapālakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1087\.

::gatha1
‘‘Uccamidaṃ maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ…pe… vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.

::hangnum
1089\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
1090\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:V:0.0073} manussesu manussabhūto, ahosiṃ yavapālako;
::

::gathalast
Addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1091\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:P:0.0107} adāsahaṃ bhāgaṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Kummāsapiṇḍaṃ datvāna, modāmi nandane vane.
::

::hangnum
1092\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena {pb:M:0.0100} metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Yavapālakavimānaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Paṭhamakuṇḍalīvimānavatthu

1095\.

::

::gathalast

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1

::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, rañño pāyāsissa ahosiṃ māṇavo;
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::centre
(Uttara) pāyāsivimānaṃ {note:uttaravimānaṃ (sī. syā. aṭṭha.)} dasamaṃ.
::

Pāyāsivaggo chaṭṭho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha2
Dve agārino phaladāyī, dve upassayadāyī bhikkhāya dāyī;
::

::gathalast
Yavapālako ceva dve, kuṇḍalino pāyāsīti {note:pāṭhabhedo natthi};
::

::gathalast
Purisānaṃ dutiyo vaggo pavuccatīti.
::

#### 4. Suvaṇṇavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇamaye {pb:P:0.0114} pabbatasmiṃ, vimānaṃ sabbatopabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hemajālapaṭicchannaṃ {note:hemajālakapacchannaṃ (sī.)}, kiṅkiṇi {note:kiṅkaṇika (syā. ka.), kiṅkiṇika (pī.)} jālakappitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1135\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhaṃsā sukatā thambhā, sabbe veḷuriyāmayā;
::

::gathalast
Ekamekāya aṃsiyā, ratanā satta nimmitā.
::

::hangnum
1136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Veḷuriyasuvaṇṇassa, phalikā rūpiyassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Masāragallamuttāhi, lohitaṅgamaṇīhi ca.
::

::hangnum
1137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Citrā manoramā bhūmi, na tatthuddhaṃsatī rajo;
::

::gathalast
Gopāṇasīgaṇā pītā, kūṭaṃ dhārenti nimmitā.
::

::hangnum
1138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sopāṇāni {pb:V:0.0077} ca cattāri, nimmitā caturo disā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanagabbhehi{pb:T:0.0130}, ādiccova virocati.
::

::hangnum
1139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vediyā catasso tattha, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
::

::gathalast
Daddallamānā ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
::

::hangnum
1140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ vimāne pavare, devaputto mahappabho;
::

::gathalast
Atirocasi vaṇṇena, udayantova bhāṇumā.
::

::hangnum
1141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānassa {pb:M:0.0106} te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
::

::gathalast
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
::

::hangnum
1142\.
::

::gatha1
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ andhakavindasmiṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
::

::gathalast
Vihāraṃ satthu kāresiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
1144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha gandhañca mālañca, paccayañca {note:paccaggañca (sī.), paccagghañca (?)} vilepanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Vihāraṃ satthu adāsiṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Tena mayhaṃ idaṃ laddhaṃ, vasaṃ vattemi nandane.
::

::hangnum
1145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandane ca vane {note:nandane pavane (sī. syā.)} ramme, nānādijagaṇāyute;
::

::gathalast
Ramāmi naccagītehi, accharāhi purakkhato’’ti.
::

::centre
Suvaṇṇavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1154\.
::

1155\.

::hangnum

#### 6. Gopālavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1159\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvāna devaṃ paṭipucchi bhikkhu, ucce vimānamhi ciraṭṭhitike;
::

::gathalast
Āmuttahatthābharaṇaṃ yasassiṃ {note:āmuttahatthābharaṇo yasassī (syā. pī. ka.)}, dibbe vimānamhi yathāpi candimā.
::

::hangnum
1160\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alaṅkato {pb:M:0.0108}{pb:P:0.0117} malyadharo {note:mālabhārī (sī.), māladharī (ka.)} suvattho, sukuṇḍalī kappitakesamassu;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1161\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ, aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā;
::

::gathalast
