::

::hangnum
1162\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1163\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:T:0.0133} devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, saṅgamma rakkhissaṃ paresaṃ dhenuyo;
::

::gathalast
Tato ca āgā samaṇo mamantike gāvo ca māse agamaṃsu khādituṃ.
::

::hangnum
1165\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dvayajja {pb:V:0.0079} kiccaṃ ubhayañca kāriyaṃ, iccevahaṃ {note:iccevaṃ (ka.)} bhante tadā vicintayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato ca saññaṃ paṭiladdhayoniso, dadāmi bhanteti khipiṃ anantakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1166\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So māsakhettaṃ turito avāsariṃ, purā ayaṃ bhañjati yassidaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato ca kaṇho urago mahāviso, aḍaṃsi pāde turitassa me sato.
::

::hangnum
1167\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāhaṃ {pb:M:0.0109} aṭṭomhi dukkhena pīḷito, bhikkhu ca taṃ sāmaṃ muñcitvānantakaṃ {note:muñcitva nantakaṃ (sī.), muñcitvā anantakaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Ahāsi kummāsaṃ mamānukampayā {note:mamānukampiyā (pī. ka.), mamānukampāya (syā.)}, tato cuto kālakatomhi devatā.
::

::hangnum
1168\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva {pb:T:0.0134} kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhipādayāmi taṃ.
::

::hangnum
1169\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadevake loke samārake ca, añño muni natthi tayānukampako;
::

::gathalast
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhivādayāmi taṃ.
::

::hangnum
1170\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmiṃ {pb:P:0.0118} loke parasmiṃ vā pana, añño munī natthi tayānukampako;
::

::gathalast
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhivādayāmi ta’’nti.
::

::centre
Gopālavimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Kaṇḍakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1171\.

::gatha1
‘‘Puṇṇamāse yathā cando, nakkhattaparivārito;

1172\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
1173\.

::gatha1
‘‘Veḷuriyasuvaṇṇassa, phalikā rūpiyassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Masāragallamuttāhi, lohitaṅgamaṇīhi ca.
::

::hangnum
1174\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Citrā manoramā bhūmi, veḷūriyassa santhatā;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārā {pb:T:0.0135} subhā rammā, pāsādo te sumāpito.
::

::hangnum
1175\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rammā {pb:M:0.0110}{pb:P:0.0119} ca te pokkharaṇī, puthulomanisevitā;
::

::gathalast
Acchodakā vippasannā, sovaṇṇavālukasanthatā.
::

::hangnum
1176\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nānāpadumasañchannā, puṇḍarīkasamotatā {note:samotthatā (ka.), samogatā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Surabhiṃ sampavāyanti, manuññā māluteritā.
::

::hangnum
1177\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā {pb:V:0.0080} te ubhato passe, vanagumbā sumāpitā;
::

::gathalast
Upetā puppharukkhehi, phalarukkhehi cūbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1178\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇapāde pallaṅke, muduke goṇakatthate {note:colasanthate (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nisinnaṃ devarājaṃva, upatiṭṭhanti accharā.
::

::hangnum
1179\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbābharaṇasañchannā, nānāmālāvibhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Ramenti taṃ mahiddhikaṃ, vasavattīva modasi.
::

::hangnum
1180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bherisaṅkhamudiṅgāhi, vīṇāhi paṇavehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Ramasi ratisampanno, naccagīte suvādite.
::

::hangnum
1181\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibbā te vividhā rūpā, dibbā saddā atho rasā;
::

::gathalast
Gandhā ca te adhippetā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā.
::

::hangnum
1182\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ vimāne pavare, devaputta mahappabho;
::

::gathalast
Atirocasi vaṇṇena, udayantova bhāṇumā.
::

::hangnum
1183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānassa te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
::

::gathalast
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
::

::hangnum
1184\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:T:0.0136} devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ kapilavatthusmiṃ, sākiyānaṃ puruttame;
::

::gathalast
Suddhodanassa puttassa, kaṇḍako sahajo ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā so aḍḍharattāyaṃ, bodhāya mabhinikkhami;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ mudūhi pāṇīhi, jāli {note:jāla (sī.)} tambanakhehi ca.
::

::hangnum
1187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satthiṃ ākoṭayitvāna, vaha sammāti cabravi;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ lokaṃ tārayissaṃ, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:0.0111} me giraṃ suṇantassa, hāso me vipulo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto sumano, abhisīsiṃ {note:abhisiṃsiṃ (sī.), abhisīsi (pī.)} tadā ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1189\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhirūḷhañca maṃ ñatvā, sakyaputtaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto mudito, vahissaṃ purisuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1190\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paresaṃ vijitaṃ gantvā, uggatasmiṃ divākare {note:divaṅkare (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mamaṃ channañca ohāya, anapekkho so apakkami.
::

::hangnum
1191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:P:0.0120} tambanakhe pāde, jivhāya parilehisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gacchantañca mahāvīraṃ, rudamāno udikkhisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adassanenahaṃ {pb:V:0.0081} tassa, sakyaputtassa sirīmato;
::

::gathalast
Alatthaṃ garukābādhaṃ, khippaṃ me maraṇaṃ ahu.
::

::hangnum
1193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasseva ānubhāvena, vimānaṃ āvasāmidaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmaguṇopetaṃ{pb:T:0.0137}, dibbaṃ devapuramhi ca.
::

::hangnum
1194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañca me ahuvā hāso, saddaṃ sutvāna bodhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Teneva kusalamūlena, phusissaṃ āsavakkhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1195\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi bhante gaccheyyāsi, satthu buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Mamāpi naṃ vacanena, sirasā vajjāsi vandanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1196\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi daṭṭhuṃ gacchissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dullabhaṃ dassanaṃ hoti, lokanāthāna tādina’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1197\.
::

::gatha1
So kataññū katavedī, satthāraṃ upasaṅkami;
::

::gathalast

::

::gathalast

::centre

#### 8. Anekavaṇṇavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1199\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anekavaṇṇaṃ {pb:M:0.0112}{pb:P:0.0121} darasokanāsanaṃ, vimānamāruyha anekacittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parivārito accharāsaṅgaṇena, sunimmito bhūtapatīva modasi.
::

::hangnum
1200\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samassamo natthi kuto panuttaro {note:uttari (ka.)}, yasena puññena ca iddhiyā ca;
::

::gatha2
Sabbe ca devā tidasagaṇā samecca, taṃ {pb:T:0.0138} taṃ namassanti sasiṃva devā;
::

::gathalast
Imā ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
::

::hangnum
1201\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi {pb:P:0.0122} mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1202\.
::

::gatha1
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1203\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ bhadante ahuvāsi pubbe, sumedhanāmassa jinassa sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Puthujjano ananubodhohamasmi {note:anavabodhohamasmiṃ (sī.), ananubodhohamāsiṃ (?)}, so satta vassāni paribbajissahaṃ {note:pabbajissahaṃ (syā. ka.), pabbajisāhaṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
1204\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ {pb:V:0.0082} sumedhassa jinassa satthuno, parinibbutassoghatiṇṇassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Ratanuccayaṃ hemajālena channaṃ, vanditvā thūpasmiṃ manaṃ pasādayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1205\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:0.0113} māsi dānaṃ na ca matthi dātuṃ, pare ca kho tattha samādapesiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pūjetha naṃ pūjanīyassa {note:pūjaneyyassa (syā. ka.)} dhātuṃ, evaṃ {pb:T:0.0139} kira saggamito gamissatha.
::

::hangnum
1206\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca dibbaṃ anubhomi attanā;
::

::gathalast
Modāmahaṃ tidasagaṇassa majjhe, na tassa puññassa khayampi ajjhaga’’nti.
::

::centre
Anekavaṇṇavimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 9. Maṭṭhakuṇḍalīvimānavatthu

::hangnum
1207\.
::

::gatha1
{note:pe. va. 186} ‘‘Alaṅkato {pb:P:0.0123} maṭṭhakuṇḍalī {note:maṭṭakuṇḍalī (sī.)}, māladhārī haricandanussado;
::

::gathalast
Bāhā paggayha kandasi, vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuva’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1208\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayo pabhassaro, uppanno rathapañjaro mama;
::

::gathalast
Tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi, tena dukkhena jahāmi {note:jahissaṃ (sī.), jahissāmi (syā. pī.)} jīvita’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1209\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇimayaṃ, lohitakamayaṃ {note:lohitaṅgamayaṃ (syā.), lohitaṅkamayaṃ (sī.), lohamayaṃ (katthaci)} atha rūpiyamayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ācikkha {note:ācikkhatha (ka.)} me bhaddamāṇava, cakkayugaṃ paṭipādayāmi te’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1210\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:T:0.0140} māṇavo tassa pāvadi, ‘‘candimasūriyā ubhayettha dissare;
::

::gathalast
Sovaṇṇamayo ratho mama, tena cakkayugena sobhatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1211\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bālo {pb:M:0.0114} kho tvaṃ asi māṇava, yo tvaṃ patthayase apatthiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi tuvaṃ marissasi, na hi tvaṃ lacchasi candimasūriye’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1212\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gamanāgamanampi dissati, vaṇṇadhātu ubhayattha vīthiyā;
::

::gathalast
Peto {note:peto pana (sī. syā.)} kālakato na dissati, ko nidha kandataṃ bālyataro’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1213\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ kho vadesi māṇava, ahameva kandataṃ bālyataro;
::

::gathalast
Candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ, petaṃ kālakatābhipatthayi’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1214\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
::

::hangnum
1215\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abbahī {pb:T:0.0141} {note:abbūḷha (pī.), abbūḷhaṃ (syā. ka.)} vata me sallaṃ, sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
1216\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāhaṃ {pb:V:0.0083}{pb:P:0.0124} abbūḷhasallosmi, sītibhūtosmi nibbuto;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, vata sutvāna māṇavāti.
::

::hangnum
1217\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu {note:ādu (sī. syā.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1218\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañca {note:yaṃ (ka.)} kandasi yañca rodasi, puttaṃ āḷāhane sayaṃ dahitvā;
::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvā kammaṃ, tidasānaṃ sahabyataṃ gato’’ti {note:pattoti (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
1219\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appaṃ {pb:M:0.0115} vā bahuṃ vā nāddasāma, dānaṃ dadantassa sake agāre;
::

::gathalast
Uposathakammaṃ vā {note:uposathakammañca (ka.)} tādisaṃ, kena kammena gatosi devaloka’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1220\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ābādhikohaṃ dukkhito gilāno, āturarūpomhi sake nivesane;
::

::gathalast
Buddhaṃ vigatarajaṃ vitiṇṇakaṅkhaṃ, addakkhiṃ sugataṃ anomapaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1221\ .
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāhaṃ muditamano pasannacitto, añjaliṃ {pb:T:0.0142} akariṃ tathāgatassa;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvāna kammaṃ, tidasānaṃ sahabyataṃ gato’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1222\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Acchariyaṃ vata abbhutaṃ vata, añjalikammassa ayamīdiso vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi muditamano pasannacitto, ajjeva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vajāmī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1223\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjeva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vajāhi, dhammañca saṅghañca pasannacitto;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva sikkhāya padāni pañca, akhaṇḍaphullāni samādiyassu.
::

::hangnum
1224\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viramassu khippaṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayassu;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapo mā ca musā bhaṇāhi, sakena dārena ca hohi tuṭṭho’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1225\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthakāmosi me yakkha, hitakāmosi devate;
::

::gathalast
Karomi tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ, tvaṃsi ācariyo mamāti.
::

::hangnum
1226\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upemi saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ, dhammañcāpi anuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghañca naradevassa, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1227\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇātipātā {pb:M:0.0116}{pb:P:0.0125} viramāmi khippaṃ, loke {pb:T:0.0143} adinnaṃ parivajjayāmi;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapo no ca musā bhaṇāmi, sakena dārena ca homi tuṭṭho’’ti.
::

::centre
Maṭṭhakuṇḍalīvimānaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Serīsakavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1228\.
::

::gatha1
{note:pe. va. 604} Suṇotha {pb:V:0.0084}{pb:P:0.0126} yakkhassa ca vāṇijāna ca, samāgamo yattha tadā ahosi;
::

::gathalast
Yathā kathaṃ itaritarena cāpi, subhāsitaṃ tañca suṇātha sabbe.
::

::hangnum
1229\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo so ahu rājā pāyāsi nāma {note:nāmo (sī.)}, bhummānaṃ sahabyagato yasassī;
::

::gathalast
So modamānova sake vimāne, amānuso mānuse ajjhabhāsīti.
::

::hangnum
1230\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaṅke araññe amanussaṭṭhāne, kantāre appodake appabhakkhe;
::

::gathalast
Suduggame vaṇṇupathassa majjhe, vaṅkaṃ bhayā {note:dhaṅkaṃbhayā (ka.)} naṭṭhamanā manussā.
::

::hangnum
1231\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nayidha phalā mūlamayā ca santi, upādānaṃ natthi kutodha bhakkho;
::

::gathalast
Aññatra paṃsūhi ca vālukāhi ca, tatāhi {pb:T:0.0144} uṇhāhi ca dāruṇāhi ca.
::

::hangnum
1232\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ujjaṅgalaṃ tattamivaṃ kapālaṃ, anāyasaṃ paralokena tulyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Luddānamāvāsamidaṃ purāṇaṃ, bhūmippadeso abhisattarūpo.
::

::hangnum
1233\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha {pb:M:0.0117} tumhe kena {note:kena nu (syā. ka.)} vaṇṇena, kimāsamānā imaṃ padesaṃ hi;
::

::gathalast
Anupaviṭṭhā sahasā samecca, lobhā bhayā atha vā sampamūḷhā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1234\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Magadhesu aṅgesu ca satthavāhā, āropayitvā paṇiyaṃ puthuttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te yāmase sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ patthayānā.
::

::hangnum
1235\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Divā {pb:P:0.0127} pipāsaṃ nadhivāsayantā, yoggānukampañca samekkhamānā,
::

::gathalast
Etena vegena āyāma sabbe {note:sabbe te (ka.)}, rattiṃ maggaṃ paṭipannā vikāle.
::

::hangnum
1236\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te duppayātā aparaddhamaggā, andhākulā vippanaṭṭhā araññe;
::

::gathalast
Suduggame {pb:T:0.0145} vaṇṇupathassa majjhe, disaṃ na jānāma pamūḷhacittā.
::

::hangnum
1237\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca disvāna adiṭṭhapubbaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhañca tavañca yakkha;
::

::gathalast
Tatuttariṃ jīvitamāsamānā, disvā patītā sumanā udaggā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1238\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāraṃ samuddassa imañca vaṇṇuṃ {note:vanaṃ (syā.), vaṇṇaṃ (ka.)}, vettācaraṃ {note:vettaṃ paraṃ (syā.), vettācāraṃ (ka.)} saṅkupathañca maggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nadiyo pana pabbatānañca duggā, puthuddisā gacchatha bhogahetu.
::

::hangnum
1239\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pakkhandiyāna vijitaṃ paresaṃ, verajjake mānuse pekkhamānā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ vo sutaṃ vā atha vāpi diṭṭhaṃ, accherakaṃ taṃ vo suṇoma tātā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1240\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Itopi {pb:M:0.0118} accherataraṃ kumāra, na to sutaṃ vā atha vāpi diṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atītamānussakameva sabbaṃ, disvāna tappāma anomavaṇṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1241\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vehāyasaṃ pokkharañño savanti, pahūtamalyā {pb:T:0.0146} {note:pahūtamālyā (syā.)} bahupuṇḍarīkā;
::

::gathalast
Dumā cime {note:dumā ca te (syā. ka.)} niccaphalūpapannā, atīva gandhā surabhiṃ pavāyanti.
::

::hangnum
1242\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Veḷūriyathambhā {pb:V:0.0085} satamussitāse, silāpavāḷassa ca āyataṃsā;
::

::gathalast
Masāragallā sahalohitaṅgā, thambhā ime jotirasāmayāse.
::

::hangnum
1243\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassathambhaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ, tesūpari sādhumidaṃ vimānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ratanantaraṃ kañcanavedimissaṃ, tapanīyapaṭṭehi ca sādhuchannaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1244\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jambonaduttattamidaṃ sumaṭṭho, pāsādasopāṇaphalūpapanno;
::

::gathalast
Daḷho ca vaggu ca susaṅgato ca {note:vaggu sumukho susaṅgato (sī.)}, atīva nijjhānakhamo manuñño.
::

::hangnum
1245\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratanantarasmiṃ {pb:P:0.0128} bahuannapānaṃ, parivārito accharāsaṅgaṇena;
::

::gathalast
Murajaālambaratūriyaghuṭṭho, abhivanditosi thutivandanāya.
::

::hangnum
1246\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:T:0.0147} modasi nārigaṇappabodhano, vimānapāsādavare manorame;
::

::gathalast
Acintiyo sabbaguṇūpapanno, rājā yathā vessavaṇo naḷinyā {note:naḷiññaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1247\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devo {pb:M:0.0119} nu āsi udavāsi yakkho, udāhu devindo manussabhūto;
::

::gathalast
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, ācikkha ko nāma tuvaṃsi yakkho’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1248\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Serīsako {note:serissako (sī. syā.)} nāma ahamhi yakkho, kantāriyo vaṇṇupathamhi gutto;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ padesaṃ abhipālayāmi, vacanakaro vessavaṇassa rañño’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1249\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhiccaladdhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te, sayaṃ kataṃ udāhu devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, kathaṃ tayā laddhamidaṃ manuñña’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1250\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nādhiccaladdhaṃ na pariṇāmajaṃ me, na sayaṃ kataṃ na hi devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakehi kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi {pb:T:0.0148} me laddhamidaṃ manuñña’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1251\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, kathaṃ tayā laddhamidaṃ vimāna’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1252\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mamaṃ pāyāsīti ahu samaññā, rajjaṃ yadā kārayiṃ kosalānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Natthikadiṭṭhi kadariyo pāpadhammo, ucchedavādī ca tadā ahosiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1253\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇo ca kho āsi kumārakassapo, bahussuto cittakathī uḷāro;
::

::gathalast
So me tadā dhammakathaṃ abhāsi {note:akāsi (sī.)}, diṭṭhivisūkāni vinodayī me.
::

::hangnum
1254\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāhaṃ {pb:M:0.0120} tassa {note:tāhaṃ (ka.)} dhammakathaṃ suṇitvā, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayissaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Pāṇātipātā virato ahosiṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayissaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapo {pb:P:0.0129} no ca musā abhāṇiṃ, sakena dārena ca ahosi tuṭṭho.
::

::hangnum
1255\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:T:0.0149} me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Teheva kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimāna’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1256\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ {pb:V:0.0086} kirāhaṃsu narā sapaññā, anaññathā vacanaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yahiṃ yahiṃ gacchati puññakammo, tahiṃ tahiṃ modati kāmakāmī.
::

::hangnum
1257\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yahiṃ yahiṃ sokapariddavo ca, vadho ca bandho ca parikkileso;
::

::gathalast
Tahiṃ tahiṃ gacchati pāpakammo, na muccati duggatiyā kadācī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1258\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammūḷharūpova jano ahosi, asmiṃ muhutte kalalīkatova;
::

::gathalast
Janassimassa tuyhañca kumāra, appaccayo kena nu kho ahosī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1259\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime ca sirīsavanā {note:ime sirīsūpavanā ca (sī.), imepi sirīsavanā ca (pī. ka.)} tātā, dibbā {note:dibbā ca (pī. ka.)} gandhā surabhī {note:surabhiṃ (sī. ka.)} sampavanti {note:sampavāyanti (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Te sampavāyanti imaṃ vimānaṃ, divā {pb:T:0.0150} ca ratto ca tamaṃ nihantvā.
::

::hangnum
1260\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imesañca {pb:M:0.0121} kho vassasataccayena, sipāṭikā phalati ekamekā;
::

::gathalast
Mānussakaṃ vassasataṃ atītaṃ, yadagge kāyamhi idhūpapanno.
::

::hangnum
1261\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvānahaṃ vassasatāni pañca, asmiṃ vimāne ṭhatvāna tātā;
::

::gathalast
Āyukkhayā puññakkhayā cavissaṃ, teneva sokena pamucchitosmī’’ti {note:samucchitosmīti (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1262\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu soceyya tathāvidho so, laddhā vimānaṃ atulaṃ cirāya;
::

::gathalast
Ye cāpi kho ittaramupapannā, te nūna soceyyuṃ parittapuññā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1263\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anucchaviṃ ovadiyañca me taṃ, yaṃ maṃ tumhe peyyavācaṃ vadetha;
::

::gathalast
Tumhe ca kho tātā mayānuguttā, yenicchakaṃ tena paletha sotthi’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1264\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gantvā {pb:P:0.0130} mayaṃ sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ patthayānā;
::

::gathalast
Yathāpayogā paripuṇṇacāgā, kāhāma {pb:T:0.0151} serīsamahaṃ uḷāra’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1265\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā ceva serīsamahaṃ akattha, sabbañca vo bhavissati yaṃ vadetha;
::

::gathalast
Pāpāni kammāni vivajjayātha, dhammānuyogañca adhiṭṭhahātha.
::

::hangnum
1266\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāsako atthi imamhi saṅghe, bahussuto sīlavatūpapanno;
::

::gathalast
Saddho ca cāgī ca supesalo ca, vicakkhaṇo santusito mutīmā.
::

::hangnum
1267\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sañjānamāno {pb:M:0.0122} na musā bhaṇeyya, parūpaghātāya na cetayeyya;
::

::gathalast
Vebhūtikaṃ pesuṇaṃ no kareyya, saṇhañca vācaṃ sakhilaṃ bhaṇeyya.
::

::hangnum
1268\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sagāravo sappaṭisso vinīto, apāpako adhisīle visuddho;
::

::gathalast
So mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi jantu, dhammena poseti ariyavutti.
::

::hangnum
1269\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maññe so mātāpitūnaṃ kāraṇā, bhogāni pariyesati na attahetu;
::

::gathalast
Mātāpitūnañca yo {note:so (?)} accayena, nekkhammapoṇo {pb:T:0.0152} carissati brahmacariyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1270\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ujū avaṅko asaṭho amāyo, na lesakappena ca vohareyya;
::

::gathalast
So tādiso sukatakammakārī, dhamme ṭhito kinti labhetha dukkhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1271\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:V:0.0087} kāraṇā pātukatomhi attanā, tasmā dhammaṃ passatha vāṇijāse;
::

::gatha2
Aññatra teniha bhasmī {note:bhasmi (syā.), bhasma (ka.)} bhavetha, andhākulā vippanaṭṭhā araññe;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ khippamānena lahuṃ parena, sukho have sappurisena saṅgamo’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1272\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nāma so kiñca karoti kammaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Kiṃ nāmadheyyaṃ kiṃ pana tassa gottaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Mayampi naṃ daṭṭhukāmamha yakkha, yassānukampāya idhāgatosi;
::

::gathalast
Lābhā hi tassa, yassa tuvaṃ pihesī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1273\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:0.0123}{pb:P:0.0131} kappako sambhavanāmadheyyo,
::

::gatha2
Upāsako kocchaphalūpajīvī;
::

::gatha3
Jānātha naṃ tumhākaṃ pesiyo so,
::

::gathalast
Mā {pb:T:0.0153} kho naṃ hīḷittha supesalo so’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1274\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jānāmase yaṃ tvaṃ pavadesi {note:vadesi (sī.)} yakkha,
::

::gatha2
Na kho naṃ jānāma sa edisoti;
::

::gatha3
Mayampi naṃ pūjayissāma yakkha,
::

::gathalast
Sutvāna tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ uḷāra’’nti.
::

::hangnum
1275\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci imasmiṃ satthe manussā,
::

::gatha2
Daharā mahantā athavāpi majjhimā;
::

::gatha3
Sabbeva te ālambantu vimānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Passantu puññānaṃ phalaṃ kadariyā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1276\.
::

::gatha1
Te tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti,
::

::gatha2
Taṃ kappakaṃ tattha purakkhatvā {note:purakkhipitvā (sī.)};
::

::gatha3
Sabbeva te ālambiṃsu vimānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa.
::

::hangnum
1277\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:T:0.0154} tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayiṃsu;
::

::gatha2
Pāṇātipātā viratā ahesuṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayiṃsu;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapā no ca musā bhaṇiṃsu, sakena dārena ca ahesuṃ tuṭṭhā.
::

::hangnum
1278\.
::

::gatha1
Te tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayitvā;
::

::gathalast
Pakkāmi sattho anumodamāno, yakkhiddhiyā anumato punappunaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1279\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gantvāna {pb:M:0.0124} te sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ {note:udaya (pī. ka.)} patthayānā;
::

::gathalast
Yathāpayogā paripuṇṇalābhā, paccāgamuṃ pāṭaliputtamakkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
1280\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gantvāna {pb:V:0.0088} te saṅgharaṃ sotthivanto,
::

::gatha2
Puttehi dārehi samaṅgibhūtā;
::

::gatha3
Ānandī vittā {note:ānandacittā (syā.), ānandīcittā (ka.)} sumanā patītā,
::

::gatha2
Akaṃsu serīsamahaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Serīsakaṃ te pariveṇaṃ māpayiṃsu.
::

::hangnum
1281\.
::

::gatha1
Etādisā sappurisāna sevanā,
::

::gatha2
Mahatthikā dhammaguṇāna sevanā;
::

::gatha3
Ekassa atthāya upāsakassa,
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva sattā sukhitā {note:sukhino (pī. ka.)} ahesunti.
::

::centre
Serīsakavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

#### 11. Sunikkhittavimānavatthu

::hangnum
1282\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uccamidaṃ {pb:P:0.0134} maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgārā {pb:T:0.0155} sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
::

::hangnum
1283\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
::

::hangnum
1284\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
1285\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi {pb:M:0.0125} ‘taṃ deva mahānubhāva, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::hangnum
1286\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:P:0.0135} devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1287\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dunnikkhittaṃ mālaṃ sunikkhipitvā, patiṭṭhapetvā sugatassa thūpe;
::

::gathalast
Mahiddhiko camhi mahānubhāvo, dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto.
::

::hangnum
1288\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo,
::

::gatha2
Tena me idha mijjhati;
::

::gatha3
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā,
::

::gathalast
Ye keci manaso piyā.
::

::hangnum
1289\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva,
::

::gatha2
Manussabhūto yamahaṃ akāsiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Tenamhi {pb:T:0.0156} evaṃ jalitānubhāvo,
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Sunikkhittavimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sunikkhittavaggo sattamo niṭṭhito.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:V:0.0089} –

::gatha1
Dve daliddā vanavihārā, bhatako gopālakaṇḍakā;
::

::gatha2
Anekavaṇṇamaṭṭhakuṇḍalī, serīsako sunikkhittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Purisānaṃ tatiyo vaggo pavuccatīti.
::

::centre
Bhāṇavāraṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::centre
Vimānavatthupāḷi niṭṭhitā.
::
